{"parentUuid":null,"isSidechain":true,"promptId":"d6863095-d53e-4d5b-8db9-e2ecc8635efc","agentId":"ae585f19a8c44725e","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":"Design the visual effects system for the document engine's graphic primitives.\n\n## Context\n\nWe store graphic primitives in `document.element` (text, rect, line, circle, ellipse, image, path, group). Each element has a `props JSONB` column for type-specific and visual properties.\n\nVisual effects are properties APPLIED TO a primitive — they don't create new types. A rect with a gradient fill is still a rect. An image with a shadow is still an image.\n\n## Scope\n\nSpec every visual effect the engine should support, organized by category. For each effect:\n- What it does visually\n- Which element types it applies to (all? specific types?)\n- How it's stored in `props JSONB` (key names, value types, defaults)\n- How it renders in SVG (exact SVG elements/attributes)\n- Priority: MUST (Phase 1) / SHOULD (Phase 2) / COULD (Phase 3)\n\n## Categories to spec\n\n### 1. Fill effects\n- Solid color fill (hex, rgba)\n- Linear gradient (angle/direction, color stops with positions)\n- Radial gradient (center, radius, color stops)\n- No fill / transparent\n- Pattern fill (future — hatching, dots)\n- Which elements support fill? (rect, circle, ellipse, path, text — NOT line, NOT image)\n\n### 2. Stroke effects\n- Solid stroke (color, width)\n- Dashed stroke (dash array patterns: dashed, dotted, dash-dot, custom)\n- No stroke\n- Stroke line cap (butt, round, square)\n- Stroke line join (miter, round, bevel)\n- Arrow heads (start, end, both — for lines and paths)\n- Which elements support stroke?\n\n### 3. Shadow effects\n- Drop shadow (offsetX, offsetY, blur, color, opacity)\n- Inner shadow (future?)\n- Which elements support shadow?\n- SVG implementation: `<feDropShadow>` vs `<feGaussianBlur>` + `<feOffset>` + `<feComposite>`\n\n### 4. Filter effects (primarily for images, but could apply to any)\n- Brightness (percentage)\n- Contrast (percentage)\n- Grayscale (percentage)\n- Blur (radius)\n- Sepia (percentage)\n- Hue rotate (degrees)\n- Saturate (percentage)\n- SVG filter chain: `<feColorMatrix>`, `<feComponentTransfer>`, `<feGaussianBlur>`\n\n### 5. Clip & mask effects\n- Rectangular clip (with border radius)\n- Circular clip\n- Custom path clip (future)\n- Opacity mask (future)\n- SVG implementation: `<clipPath>` with `<rect rx>` or `<circle>`\n\n### 6. Transform effects\n- Rotation (degrees, around element center)\n- Flip horizontal / vertical\n- Scale (uniform, non-uniform — future?)\n- SVG implementation: `transform=\"rotate(deg, cx, cy)\"`, `translate + scale + translate` for flip\n\n### 7. Border effects (primarily for images and rects)\n- Border width, color, radius (uniform)\n- Per-corner radius (future)\n- Per-side border (future — for table cells)\n- SVG: overlay `<rect fill=\"none\" stroke=... rx=...>`\n\n### 8. Opacity & blending\n- Element opacity (0-1)\n- Blend modes (multiply, screen, overlay — future?)\n\n## Current illustrator reference\n\nRead `/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench/docs/ILLUSTRATOR-GRAPHICS.md` for the exact current implementation:\n- Image filters: brightness, contrast, grayscale via `<feColorMatrix>` + `<feComponentTransfer>`\n- Image shadow: `<feDropShadow>`\n- Image clip: `<clipPath>` with `<rect>`\n- Image flip: `translate + scale + translate`\n- Image border: overlay `<rect fill=\"none\">`\n\n## Deliverable\n\nA structured spec document with:\n\n1. **Effect catalog** — every effect, its props keys, types, defaults, valid ranges\n2. **Applicability matrix** — which effects apply to which element types\n3. **SVG rendering reference** — exact SVG output for each effect\n4. **Composability** — how effects combine (filter + shadow + clip on same element)\n5. **Props JSONB schema** — the exact JSON shape stored per effect category\n\nExample props for an image with all effects:\n```json\n{\n  \"objectFit\": \"cover\",\n  \"cropX\": 0.5, \"cropY\": 0.5, \"cropZoom\": 1,\n  \"flipH\": false, \"flipV\": false,\n  \"brightness\": 100, \"contrast\": 100, \"grayscale\": 0,\n  \"borderWidth\": 2, \"borderColor\": \"#333\", \"borderRadius\": 5,\n  \"shadowX\": 3, \"shadowY\": 3, \"shadowBlur\": 5, \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\",\n  \"fill\": \"#ffffff\",\n  \"stroke\": \"#000000\", \"strokeWidth\": 0.5, \"strokeDasharray\": \"5,3\"\n}\n```\n\nBe exhaustive. This spec will be used to implement the SVG renderer in PG (document.render_svg) and the pack."},"uuid":"85451193-8908-45fe-85a3-244a08e978ae","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:38:04.670Z","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

Single-page only. No tables, no rich text, no data binding, no multi-page. Two fonts (Libre Baskerville, Source Sans 3).\n    12→\n    13→---\n    14→\n    15→## 1. Text Primitives\n    16→\n    17→Text is the foundation of every business document. The current engine has basic single-style text with word-wrap. Business and creative documents demand far more.\n    18→\n    19→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n    20→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n    21→| 1.1 | **Single-line text** | Positioned text with font, size, color, anchor | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`add_text`) |\n    22→| 1.2 | **Multi-line text (word-wrap)** | Auto-wrap to maxWidth, explicit `\\n` breaks | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`maxWidth`) |\n    23→| 1.3 | **Text alignment** | start/middle/end (horizontal anchor) | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`textAnchor`) |\n    24→| 1.4 | **Rich text spans** | Bold, italic, color changes within a single text block. E.g. \"Total: **1 480,80 EUR**\" | MUST | 1 | H | MISSING -- currently entire block shares one style |\n    25→| 1.5 | **Paragraph text** | Multi-paragraph blocks with inter-paragraph spacing, first-line indent | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING -- `\\n` exists but no paragraph-level control |\n    26→| 1.6 | **Justified text** | Full justification (left+right aligned) via Knuth-Plass or greedy algorithm | SHOULD | 2 | H | MISSING |\n    27→| 1.7 | **Multi-column text** | Text flowing across 2-3 columns (brochures, newsletters) | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    28→| 1.8 | **Bulleted lists** | Bullet character + hanging indent, nested levels | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    29→| 1.9 | **Numbered lists** | Auto-incrementing numbers/letters, nested levels | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    30→| 1.10 | **Merge fields / variables** | `{{client.name}}`, `{{facture.total}}` -- placeholder syntax resolved at generation time | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING -- currently done by orchestrator via `batch_update`, but no native support |\n    31→| 1.11 | **Text overflow: shrink-to-fit** | Auto-reduce font size if text exceeds bounding box | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    32→| 1.12 | **Text overflow: truncate + ellipsis** | Clip text with \"...\" when exceeding maxWidth | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    33→| 1.13 | **Text overflow: linked frames** | Text overflowing from one frame continues in another (multi-page) | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    34→| 1.14 | **Superscript / subscript** | For legal references (1), footnote markers, chemical formulas | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    35→| 1.15 | **Text decorations** | Underline, strikethrough, overline | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    36→| 1.16 | **RTL / BiDi text** | Right-to-left (Arabic, Hebrew), bidirectional mixing | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    37→| 1.17 | **CJK text** | Chinese/Japanese/Korean vertical and horizontal layout | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    38→| 1.18 | **Hyphenation** | Automatic word hyphenation per language rules (essential for justified text) | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    39→\n    40→### Analysis\n    41→\n    42→The biggest gap for business documents is **1.4 Rich text spans** -- every invoice needs \"Total TTC: **1 480,80 EUR**\" with the amount in bold. Without this, generating professional documents requires multiple separate text elements positioned manually, which is fragile.\n    43→\n    44→**1.10 Merge fields** is architecturally important: currently the orchestrator does batch_update after cloning a template, which works but means Claude must understand every field mapping. A native `{{variable}}` system would make templates self-documenting and enable non-AI generation pipelines.\n    45→\n    46→---\n    47→\n    48→## 2. Table Primitives\n    49→\n    50→Tables are the heart of business documents. Every invoice, quote, purchase order, and report has at least one. The current engine has **no table primitive** -- tables must be composed from individual text and line elements.\n    51→\n    52→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n    53→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n    54→| 2.1 | **Simple table** | Rows, columns, cells with text content | MUST | 1 | H | MISSING -- composed manually from text+lines |\n    55→| 2.2 | **Header row** | Distinct styling (bold, background), repeated on page break | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING |\n    56→| 2.3 | **Column widths: fixed** | Explicit width per column in mm | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING |\n    57→| 2.4 | **Column widths: proportional** | Star-sizing (`*`, `2*`, `3*`) to fill available width | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    58→| 2.5 | **Column widths: auto** | Shrink to content width | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    59→| 2.6 | **Cell alignment** | Horizontal (left, center, right) and vertical (top, middle, bottom) per cell | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING |\n    60→| 2.7 | **Cell borders** | Per-side border control (top, right, bottom, left), style (solid, dashed), width, color | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING |\n    61→| 2.8 | **Cell merge: colspan** | Cell spanning multiple columns | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    62→| 2.9 | **Cell merge: rowspan** | Cell spanning multiple rows | SHOULD | 2 | H | MISSING |\n    63→| 2.10 | **Alternating row colors** | Zebra striping for readability | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    64→| 2.11 | **Table footer row** | Summary/totals row with distinct styling | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    65→| 2.12 | **Table page break** | Table splits across pages with header repeated | MUST | 1 | H | MISSING (requires multi-page) |\n    66→| 2.13 | **Nested content in cells** | Images, sub-tables, rich text within cells | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n    67→| 2.14 | **Row grouping** | Collapsible sections within a table (report subtotals) | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n    68→| 2.15 | **Cell padding** | Inner spacing between cell border and content | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING |\n    69→\n    70→### Analysis\n    71→\n    72→Tables are the **single biggest gap** for business document generation. Building an invoice table from individual positioned text elements requires ~6 elements per row, manual Y calculation, and breaks completely on multi-page documents. A native table primitive is the highest priority addition.\n    73→\n    74→The minimum viable table needs: rows/columns, header row, fixed column widths, cell alignment, cell borders, cell padding. This alone unblocks 80% of business documents.\n    75→\n    76→---\n    77→\n    78→## 3. Shape Primitives\n    79→\n    80→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n    81→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n    82→| 3.1 | **Rectangle** | With position, size, fill, stroke, border-radius | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`add_rect` with `rx`) |\n    83→| 3.2 | **Line** | With endpoints, stroke, width | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`add_line`) |\n    84→| 3.3 | **Circle** | Center + radius, fill, stroke | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING -- can approximate with rect+rx but semantically different |\n    85→| 3.4 | **Ellipse** | Center + rx/ry | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    86→| 3.5 | **Polygon** | Arbitrary closed shape from point list | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n    87→| 3.6 | **Polyline** | Open path from point list | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n    88→| 3.7 | **Path** | SVG-style path data (M, L, C, Q, A, Z) for arbitrary shapes | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n    89→| 3.8 | **Arrow** | Line with arrowhead (start, end, or both) | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n    90→| 3.9 | **Dashed/dotted lines** | strokeDasharray equivalent (solid, dashed, dotted, dash-dot) | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n    91→| 3.10 | **Separator / divider** | Horizontal/vertical rule with optional decorations | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING -- can be done with line but no semantic meaning |\n    92→| 3.11 | **Decorative elements** | Ornaments, brackets, flourishes (predefined SVG library) | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n    93→| 3.12 | **Rounded rect variants** | Per-corner radius control (different radius per corner) | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING -- current `rx` is uniform |\n    94→| 3.13 | **Star / badge shape** | Configurable star/badge (n-points, inner/outer radius) | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n    95→\n    96→### Analysis\n    97→\n    98→The existing shapes (rect, line) cover basics. The most impactful additions for business documents are **3.8 Arrows** (for flowcharts, diagrams in reports) and **3.9 Dashed lines** (visual separators, cut lines on documents). **3.3 Circle** is a frequent need for bullet points, status indicators, and creative layouts.\n    99→\n   100→---\n   101→\n   102→## 4. Image Primitives\n   103→\n   104→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   105→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   106→| 4.1 | **Raster images** | PNG, JPEG, WebP embedding | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`add_image`) |\n   107→| 4.2 | **SVG embedding** | Inline SVG as an element (logos, icons) | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING -- logos must be raster |\n   108→| 4.3 | **Image crop** | Pan (cropX/cropY) and zoom (cropZoom) within frame | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (`objectFit`, `cropX/Y/Zoom`) |\n   109→| 4.4 | **Image filters** | Brightness, contrast, grayscale | SHOULD | 2 | M | EXISTS (`brightness`, `contrast`, `grayscale`) |\n   110→| 4.5 | **Image blur filter** | Gaussian blur (for background effects) | COULD | 3 | L | MISSING |\n   111→| 4.6 | **Image sepia / hue-rotate** | Color shift filters | COULD | 3 | L | MISSING |\n   112→| 4.7 | **Image mask: rounded rect** | Clip image to rounded rectangle | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`borderRadius`) |\n   113→| 4.8 | **Image mask: circle** | Clip image to circular shape | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING -- approximate with large borderRadius |\n   114→| 4.9 | **Image mask: custom shape** | Clip to arbitrary path or SVG shape | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n   115→| 4.10 | **Image shadow** | Drop shadow with offset, blur, color | SHOULD | 2 | L | EXISTS (`shadowX/Y/Blur/Color`) |\n   116→| 4.11 | **Image border** | Stroke around image with color and width | SHOULD | 2 | L | EXISTS (`borderWidth/Color`) |\n   117→| 4.12 | **Image flip** | Horizontal and vertical mirror | SHOULD | 2 | L | EXISTS (`flipH`, `flipV`) |\n   118→| 4.13 | **Watermark overlay** | Semi-transparent text/image overlaid on entire page | MUST | 1 | M | PARTIAL -- done via rotated text with low opacity, no dedicated primitive |\n   119→| 4.14 | **Background image** | Full-page or region background (cover, tile, stretch) | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING -- can place image at z=0 but no tiling |\n   120→| 4.15 | **QR code** | Generated QR from text/URL (payment, Factur-X, links) | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING |\n   121→| 4.16 | **Barcode: Code128** | Linear barcode for logistics, shipping labels | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   122→| 4.17 | **Barcode: EAN13** | Product barcode (retail, catalog) | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   123→| 4.18 | **Barcode: DataMatrix** | High-density 2D barcode | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   124→| 4.19 | **Image placeholder** | Named empty frame that shows dimensions/label until image is assigned | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n   125→| 4.20 | **Tiled image pattern** | Repeating image as fill for a region (textures, wallpaper) | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   126→\n   127→### Analysis\n   128→\n   129→Image handling is the strongest area of the current engine. The critical missing pieces are:\n   130→- **4.15 QR code**: Every French invoice will need a QR code for Factur-X compliance (2026-2027). Also essential for flyers/posters (link to event page).\n   131→- **4.2 SVG embedding**: Logos are almost always delivered as SVG. Requiring raster conversion loses quality and increases file size.\n   132→\n   133→---\n   134→\n   135→## 5. Layout Primitives\n   136→\n   137→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   138→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   139→| 5.1 | **Single page** | One canvas with format, orientation, background | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS |\n   140→| 5.2 | **Multi-page document** | Multiple pages in one document, page navigation | MUST | 1 | H | MISSING -- critical gap, 1 doc = 1 page today |\n   141→| 5.3 | **Page headers** | Content repeated at top of every page (logo, company name) | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING (requires multi-page) |\n   142→| 5.4 | **Page footers** | Content at bottom of every page (page numbers, date, legal) | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING (requires multi-page) |\n   143→| 5.5 | **Page numbers** | Auto-incrementing \"Page N/M\" in headers/footers | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING (requires multi-page) |\n   144→| 5.6 | **Margins** | Page margins (top, right, bottom, left) defining printable area | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING -- implicit via element positioning |\n   145→| 5.7 | **Columns layout** | 2-col, 3-col text flow within a page region | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n   146→| 5.8 | **Grid layout** | Snap grid for calendar, planning, inventory sheets | SHOULD | 2 | M | PARTIAL -- `distribute` with grid option exists |\n   147→| 5.9 | **Sections / blocks** | Named regions that flow vertically (header section, line items, totals, footer) | SHOULD | 2 | M | PARTIAL -- groups exist but don't \"flow\" |\n   148→| 5.10 | **Repeating sections** | A section template repeated for each item in a data array | MUST | 1 | H | MISSING -- manual batch_add per item today |\n   149→| 5.11 | **Page break control: keep-together** | Prevent breaking a group across pages | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING (requires multi-page) |\n   150→| 5.12 | **Page break control: break-before** | Force new page before a section | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING (requires multi-page) |\n   151→| 5.13 | **Bleed zone** | Extra area beyond trim for professional print | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (`bleed_mm` in export_pdf) |\n   152→| 5.14 | **Safe zone / inner margin** | Area inset from page edge where no content should be placed | SHOULD | 2 | L | EXISTS (`safe_margin_mm` in home_print) |\n   153→| 5.15 | **Master pages / templates** | Reusable page layout applied to multiple pages (different first page, left/right) | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n   154→| 5.16 | **Relative positioning** | Place elements relative to other elements (below, right_of, gap) | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (below, above, right_of, left_of, gap, center_h/v) |\n   155→| 5.17 | **Alignment tools** | Align multiple elements to edges or centers | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (align tool) |\n   156→| 5.18 | **Distribution tools** | Equal spacing between elements | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (distribute tool) |\n   157→| 5.19 | **Z-ordering** | Front/back/forward/backward element order | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (reorder_element) |\n   158→| 5.20 | **Groups** | Hierarchical element grouping with nested groups | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (group_elements, ungroup, add_to_group) |\n   159→| 5.21 | **Snap-to-grid** | Automatic positioning to grid coordinates | SHOULD | 2 | L | EXISTS (client-side toggle) |\n   160→| 5.22 | **Guides / rulers** | Visual guides for alignment (non-printing) | COULD | 3 | L | MISSING |\n   161→\n   162→### Analysis\n   163→\n   164→**5.2 Multi-page** is the most critical missing layout feature. Without it, a 15-line invoice works, but a 40-line invoice is impossible. Multi-page also unlocks headers, footers, page numbers, table continuation, and all the features that make documents professional.\n   165→\n   166→**5.10 Repeating sections** is the second critical gap. Currently, generating table rows requires the orchestrator to call batch_add with calculated Y positions for each row. A native repeat mechanism would be transformative for template-based generation.\n   167→\n   168→---\n   169→\n   170→## 6. Data Binding\n   171→\n   172→Data binding transforms a static design into a reusable template. The current engine has **no data binding** -- the orchestrator (Claude or script) performs all data injection via batch_update.\n   173→\n   174→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   175→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   176→| 6.1 | **Merge fields** | `{{variable.path}}` syntax in text elements, resolved at generation time | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING -- orchestrator does it manually |\n   177→| 6.2 | **Repeating sections** | `{{#each lignes}}...{{/each}}` -- repeat a group of elements for each item in an array | MUST | 1 | H | MISSING |\n   178→| 6.3 | **Conditional visibility** | `{{#if total > 0}}` -- show/hide elements or sections based on data conditions | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   179→| 6.4 | **Computed fields** | `{{sum(lignes.total_ht)}}`, `{{page_count}}` -- calculated values | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   180→| 6.5 | **Number formatting** | Currency (`1 234,56 EUR`), percentage (`20,00%`), dates (`13 mars 2026`) | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING -- done by PL/pgSQL before injection |\n   181→| 6.6 | **Locale-aware formatting** | `fr_FR`: `1 234,56`, `en_US`: `1,234.56` -- ICU-based formatting | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   182→| 6.7 | **Image binding** | `{{entreprise.logo}}` resolving to an image path/URL | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n   183→| 6.8 | **QR code binding** | `{{qr:facture.payment_url}}` generating QR from bound data | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   184→| 6.9 | **Conditional styling** | Change color/font based on data value (red if overdue, green if paid) | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   185→| 6.10 | **Data source declaration** | Template declares what data shape it expects (schema for validation) | COULD | 3 | L | MISSING |\n   186→\n   187→### Analysis\n   188→\n   189→The current approach (orchestrator does everything) works for AI-driven generation but fails for:\n   190→- **Batch generation**: Generate 200 invoices from a CSV -- no AI needed if templates self-bind\n   191→- **Non-developer users**: A template designer should see `{{client.nom}}` in the editor, not rely on Claude to know the field names\n   192→- **Validation**: A template with declared data schema can be validated before generation\n   193→\n   194→Phase 1 should at minimum support merge fields (6.1) and repeating sections (6.2). These alone cover 90% of business document automation.\n   195→\n   196→---\n   197→\n   198→## 7. Typography\n   199→\n   200→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   201→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   202→| 7.1 | **Font families** | Serif, sans-serif, monospace, custom fonts | MUST | 1 | M | PARTIAL -- 2 fonts only (Libre Baskerville, Source Sans 3) |\n   203→| 7.2 | **Font loading** | Load custom .ttf/.otf/.woff2 fonts | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING -- hardcoded font list |\n   204→| 7.3 | **Font weights** | 100 (thin) through 900 (black) | MUST | 1 | L | PARTIAL -- normal, bold, 300, 600, 700 |\n   205→| 7.4 | **Font styles** | Normal, italic, oblique | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (normal, italic) |\n   206→| 7.5 | **Line height / leading** | Space between lines in multi-line text | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING -- uses default from font metrics |\n   207→| 7.6 | **Letter spacing / tracking** | Space between characters | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n   208→| 7.7 | **Text color** | Fill color for text | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`fill`) |\n   209→| 7.8 | **Text opacity** | Transparency for text elements | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`opacity`) |\n   210→| 7.9 | **Drop shadow on text** | Shadow behind text for contrast on images | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING -- images have shadow but text doesn't |\n   211→| 7.10 | **Outline / stroke text** | Text with visible outline (titles on photo backgrounds) | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   212→| 7.11 | **Text transform** | Uppercase, lowercase, capitalize (applied at render time) | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n   213→| 7.12 | **OpenType features: ligatures** | fi, fl, ffi ligatures for professional typography | COULD | 3 | M | DEPENDS on font + opentype.js support |\n   214→| 7.13 | **OpenType features: small caps** | True small capitals (not scaled-down uppercase) | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   215→| 7.14 | **OpenType features: old-style numerals** | Text figures that blend with lowercase (for body text) | COULD | 3 | L | MISSING |\n   216→| 7.15 | **OpenType features: tabular numerals** | Fixed-width digits for aligned number columns in tables | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING -- critical for invoice amount columns |\n   217→| 7.16 | **Monospace font** | At least one mono font for codes, references, technical content | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n   218→| 7.17 | **Web font loading** | Load fonts from Google Fonts or URLs at runtime | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   219→\n   220→### Analysis\n   221→\n   222→The current 2-font system is a significant limitation for professional documents. The minimum additions needed:\n   223→- **7.5 Line height**: Without explicit control, multi-line text blocks have unpredictable height, breaking layout calculations.\n   224→- **7.15 Tabular numerals**: Invoice columns look amateur when digits don't align. This is a make-or-break detail.\n   225→- **7.16 Monospace font**: Every business document has codes (invoice numbers, SIRET, IBAN) that look better in mono.\n   226→\n   227→Font loading (7.2) is strategically important: customers will want their brand fonts.\n   228→\n   229→---\n   230→\n   231→## 8. Colors & Fills\n   232→\n   233→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   234→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   235→| 8.1 | **Solid colors (hex)** | `#FF5500`, `#333` | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS |\n   236→| 8.2 | **Solid colors (rgb/rgba)** | `rgb(255,85,0)`, `rgba(0,0,0,0.5)` | SHOULD | 2 | L | PARTIAL -- rgba in some shadow props |\n   237→| 8.3 | **Named colors** | CSS named colors (white, navy, etc.) | COULD | 3 | L | MISSING |\n   238→| 8.4 | **Linear gradient fill** | Gradient from point A to point B with color stops | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   239→| 8.5 | **Radial gradient fill** | Gradient radiating from center with color stops | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   240→| 8.6 | **Pattern fill** | Repeating pattern (hatching, dots, stripes) as fill | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   241→| 8.7 | **Opacity / transparency** | Per-element opacity control | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`opacity`) |\n   242→| 8.8 | **CMYK color space** | Colors specified in CMYK for professional print | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n   243→| 8.9 | **Color palette / swatches** | Predefined color sets for consistent design | COULD | 3 | L | MISSING |\n   244→| 8.10 | **HSL color specification** | `hsl(30, 100%, 50%)` for intuitive color manipulation | COULD | 3 | L | MISSING |\n   245→\n   246→### Analysis\n   247→\n   248→Hex colors cover 95% of business document needs. **8.4 Linear gradients** are the most impactful addition for creative documents (headers, backgrounds, decorative elements). CMYK (8.8) is only needed for professional print shops and can be deferred to Phase 3.\n   249→\n   250→---\n   251→\n   252→## 9. Print-Specific Features\n   253→\n   254→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   255→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   256→| 9.1 | **Crop marks** | Trim marks outside page box indicating cut lines | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (`crop_marks` in export_pdf) |\n   257→| 9.2 | **Registration marks** | Cross-shaped alignment marks for multi-color printing | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   258→| 9.3 | **Bleed zone** | Area beyond trim (typically 3mm) for edge-to-edge printing | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (`bleed_mm`) |\n   259→| 9.4 | **Home print mode** | Scale content within safe margins, no bleed/marks | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (`home_print`) |\n   260→| 9.5 | **PDF/A-3 compliance** | Archival PDF supporting embedded files (required for Factur-X) | MUST | 2 | H | MISSING |\n   261→| 9.6 | **Factur-X embedding** | Attach CII XML invoice data inside PDF/A-3 | MUST | 2 | H | MISSING |\n   262→| 9.7 | **Spot colors** | Named Pantone/spot colors for brand consistency | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n   263→| 9.8 | **Overprint** | Ink overprint control for trapping | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n   264→| 9.9 | **Color bar** | Color calibration strip outside trim area | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   265→| 9.10 | **Signature zone (visual)** | Named placeholder area for handwritten/digital signature | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING |\n   266→| 9.11 | **Signature zone (digital)** | PDF signature field for cryptographic signing | SHOULD | 2 | H | MISSING |\n   267→| 9.12 | **Fold marks** | Marks indicating where to fold (tri-fold brochures) | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n   268→| 9.13 | **PDF metadata** | Title, author, subject, keywords, creation date | MUST | 1 | L | MISSING |\n   269→| 9.14 | **PDF permissions** | Print/copy/edit restrictions | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   270→\n   271→### Analysis\n   272→\n   273→**9.5 PDF/A-3** and **9.6 Factur-X** are time-critical: French e-invoicing mandate begins September 2026. B2B invoices must be Factur-X (PDF/A-3 with embedded CII XML). This is a legal requirement, not a nice-to-have.\n   274→\n   275→**9.10 Signature zone** is needed for quotes (client acceptance), contracts, and delivery receipts. Even a visual placeholder (dashed box with \"Signature\" label) covers 80% of the need.\n   276→\n   277→---\n   278→\n   279→## 10. Interactivity (Digital Documents)\n   280→\n   281→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   282→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   283→| 10.1 | **Hyperlinks** | Clickable links in PDF (to URLs, emails, phone numbers) | MUST | 1 | M | MISSING |\n   284→| 10.2 | **Internal links** | Click to jump to another page/section within the document | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   285→| 10.3 | **Bookmarks / outlines** | PDF bookmark panel for navigation (chapters, sections) | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   286→| 10.4 | **Table of contents** | Auto-generated TOC with page numbers and links | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n   287→| 10.5 | **Form fields: checkbox** | Interactive checkbox in PDF | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   288→| 10.6 | **Form fields: text input** | Fillable text field in PDF | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   289→| 10.7 | **Annotations** | Sticky notes, highlights, comments | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   290→| 10.8 | **Embedded files** | Attach files to PDF (XML for Factur-X, Excel data) | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING (overlaps with 9.6) |\n   291→\n   292→### Analysis\n   293→\n   294→**10.1 Hyperlinks** are surprisingly important for business documents: clickable \"mailto:\" for customer support, clickable payment links, clickable terms-and-conditions URLs. Most PDF generators support this and users expect it.\n   295→\n   296→---\n   297→\n   298→## 11. Export Formats\n   299→\n   300→| # | Format | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   301→|---|--------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   302→| 11.1 | **SVG** | Standalone SVG with embedded images | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`export_svg`) |\n   303→| 11.2 | **PNG** | Raster snapshot at configurable DPI | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`snapshot`) |\n   304→| 11.3 | **PDF (vector)** | Vector PDF via headless Chrome | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (`export_pdf`) -- Puppeteer dependency |\n   305→| 11.4 | **PDF (native)** | Vector PDF via pdf-lib or similar (no Chrome dependency) | SHOULD | 2 | H | MISSING -- would remove heavy Puppeteer dep |\n   306→| 11.5 | **PDF/A-3** | Archival PDF for Factur-X | MUST | 2 | H | MISSING |\n   307→| 11.6 | **DOCX** | Word document export | SHOULD | 2 | M | EXISTS (`export_docx` via npm:docx) |\n   308→| 11.7 | **HTML** | Static HTML rendering of the document | COULD | 3 | M | MISSING |\n   309→| 11.8 | **Print-ready PDF** | PDF with crop marks, bleed, registration, correct color profile | SHOULD | 2 | M | PARTIAL (crop marks + bleed exist) |\n   310→\n   311→### Analysis\n   312→\n   313→The current Puppeteer-based PDF export is heavy (Chrome headless) and doesn't work in Deno/Edge environments. Moving to native PDF generation (pdf-lib, jsPDF, or similar) would reduce the deployment footprint dramatically and enable features like hyperlinks, bookmarks, and PDF/A that Puppeteer's print-to-PDF doesn't support well.\n   314→\n   315→---\n   316→\n   317→## 12. Document Operations\n   318→\n   319→| # | Operation | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   320→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   321→| 12.1 | **Create** | New blank document | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`doc_new`) |\n   322→| 12.2 | **Save / Load** | Persist and restore documents | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`doc_save`, `doc_load`) |\n   323→| 12.3 | **Duplicate / Clone** | Copy document as template instance | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`doc_duplicate`) |\n   324→| 12.4 | **Delete** | Remove document | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`doc_delete`) |\n   325→| 12.5 | **List** | Browse saved documents | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`doc_list`) |\n   326→| 12.6 | **Rename** | Change document name | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS (`doc_rename`) |\n   327→| 12.7 | **Batch generate** | Generate N documents from template + data array | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   328→| 12.8 | **PDF merge** | Concatenate multiple single-page PDFs into one file | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   329→| 12.9 | **Version history** | Track revisions, revert to previous state | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING |\n   330→| 12.10 | **Template library** | Curated collection of reusable templates | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING -- templates are just documents today |\n   331→| 12.11 | **Lock elements** | Prevent accidental modification of certain elements | SHOULD | 2 | L | MISSING |\n   332→\n   333→---\n   334→\n   335→## 13. Measurement & Positioning\n   336→\n   337→| # | Primitive | Description | Priority | Phase | Complexity | Current State |\n   338→|---|-----------|-------------|----------|-------|------------|---------------|\n   339→| 13.1 | **Absolute positioning (mm)** | x, y coordinates in millimeters | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS |\n   340→| 13.2 | **Relative positioning** | below, above, right_of, left_of with gap | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS |\n   341→| 13.3 | **Center on canvas** | center_h, center_v | MUST | 1 | L | EXISTS |\n   342→| 13.4 | **Text measurement** | Measure text dimensions before placing | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (`measure_text`) |\n   343→| 13.5 | **Bounding box** | Computed bbox for any element | MUST | 1 | M | EXISTS (internal) |\n   344→| 13.6 | **Layout analysis** | Collision detection, bleed violations, spacing check | SHOULD | 2 | M | EXISTS (`check_layout`) |\n   345→| 13.7 | **Percentage positioning** | Position at 50% of page width instead of absolute mm | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   346→| 13.8 | **Anchoring** | Anchor element to page edge (bottom-right, etc.) | SHOULD | 2 | M | MISSING |\n   347→| 13.9 | **Constraint-based layout** | \"This element should always be 10mm below that one\" (maintained through updates) | COULD | 3 | H | MISSING -- relative positioning is one-shot at creation |\n   348→\n   349→---\n   350→\n   351→## Priority Matrix Summary\n   352→\n   353→### Phase 1 -- MVP (Business Document Generation)\n   354→\n   355→The minimum set to generate a professional invoice, quote, or purchase order.\n   356→\n   357→| Category | Must-Have Primitives |\n   358→|----------|---------------------|\n   359→| **Text** | Rich text spans (1.4), merge fields (1.10) |\n   360→| **Tables** | Simple table with headers, fixed widths, alignment, borders, padding (2.1-2.7, 2.15) |\n   361→| **Layout** | Multi-page (5.2), page headers/footers (5.3-5.4), page numbers (5.5), margins (5.6), repeating sections (5.10) |\n   362→| **Images** | QR code generation (4.15) |\n   363→| **Typography** | Line height control (7.5), at least 1 more sans-serif + 1 monospace font (7.1) |\n   364→| **Print** | Signature zone visual (9.10), PDF metadata (9.13) |\n   365→| **Interactive** | Hyperlinks in PDF (10.1) |\n   366→| **Data** | Merge fields (6.1), repeating sections (6.2), number formatting (6.5) |\n   367→\n   368→### Phase 2 -- Professional\n   369→\n   370→| Category | Key Additions |\n   371→|----------|---------------|\n   372→| **Text** | Paragraph text (1.5), justified text (1.6), bulleted/numbered lists (1.8-1.9), superscript/subscript (1.14), decorations (1.15) |\n   373→| **Tables** | Proportional/auto widths (2.4-2.5), cell merge (2.8-2.9), alternating rows (2.10), table footer (2.11), page break with header repeat (2.12) |\n   374→| **Shapes** | Circle (3.3), arrow (3.8), dashed lines (3.9) |\n   375→| **Images** | SVG embedding (4.2) |\n   376→| **Layout** | Page break control (5.11-5.12), sections/blocks (5.9) |\n   377→| **Typography** | Custom font loading (7.2), letter spacing (7.6), text shadow (7.9), outline text (7.10), tabular numerals (7.15) |\n   378→| **Colors** | Linear gradient (8.4) |\n   379→| **Print** | PDF/A-3 + Factur-X (9.5-9.6), registration marks (9.2), fold marks (9.12) |\n   380→| **Interactive** | Bookmarks (10.3), embedded files (10.8) |\n   381→| **Data** | Conditional visibility (6.3), computed fields (6.4), locale formatting (6.6) |\n   382→| **Export** | Native PDF generation (11.4), batch generate (12.7), PDF merge (12.8) |\n   383→\n   384→### Phase 3 -- Advanced\n   385→\n   386→| Category | Key Additions |\n   387→|----------|---------------|\n   388→| **Text** | Multi-column text (1.7), linked text frames (1.13), RTL/BiDi (1.16), CJK (1.17), hyphenation (1.18) |\n   389→| **Tables** | Nested content in cells (2.13), row grouping (2.14) |\n   390→| **Shapes** | Polygon/polyline/path (3.5-3.7), decorative elements (3.11) |\n   391→| **Images** | Custom shape masks (4.9), tiled patterns (4.20) |\n   392→| **Layout** | Column layout (5.7), master pages (5.15), constraint-based layout (13.9) |\n   393→| **Typography** | OpenType features (7.12-7.14), web font loading (7.17) |\n   394→| **Colors** | CMYK (8.8), pattern fills (8.6) |\n   395→| **Print** | Spot colors (9.7), overprint (9.8) |\n   396→| **Interactive** | Table of contents (10.4), form fields (10.5-10.6) |\n   397→| **Data** | Conditional styling (6.9), data source declaration (6.10) |\n   398→\n   399→---\n   400→\n   401→## Gap Analysis: Current Engine vs. Business Document Requirements\n   402→\n   403→### Critical Gaps (blocks basic invoice/quote generation)\n   404→\n   405→| Gap | Impact | Effort |\n   406→|-----|--------|--------|\n   407→| **No multi-page** | Cannot generate invoices >1 page, no headers/footers/page numbers | HIGH |\n   408→| **No tables** | Must compose from individual elements (fragile, no reflow) | HIGH |\n   409→| **No rich text** | Cannot mix bold/normal in same text block | MEDIUM |\n   410→| **No merge fields** | Template filling requires Claude to know every field | MEDIUM |\n   411→| **No QR codes** | Missing for Factur-X compliance and modern documents | MEDIUM |\n   412→\n   413→### Important Gaps (blocks professional quality)\n   414→\n   415→| Gap | Impact | Effort |\n   416→|-----|--------|--------|\n   417→| **2 fonts only** | Cannot match brand guidelines | LOW-MEDIUM |\n   418→| **No line height control** | Unpredictable multi-line layout | LOW |\n   419→| **No hyperlinks in PDF** | No clickable URLs/emails | MEDIUM |\n   420→| **No PDF/A-3** | Cannot generate Factur-X invoices (legal requirement Sept 2026) | HIGH |\n   421→| **No native PDF** | Depends on Puppeteer/Chrome -- heavy, not Edge-compatible | HIGH |\n   422→\n   423→### Strategic Gaps (blocks product differentiation)\n   424→\n   425→| Gap | Impact | Effort |\n   426→|-----|--------|--------|\n   427→| **No batch generation** | Cannot generate 200 invoices at once without AI | MEDIUM |\n   428→| **No template library** | Customers must build every template from scratch | LOW |\n   429→| **No conditional visibility** | Cannot hide/show sections based on data | MEDIUM |\n   430→| **No gradient fills** | Creative documents look flat | MEDIUM |\n   431→\n   432→---\n   433→\n   434→## Architectural Recommendation\n   435→\n   436→### Document Model Evolution\n   437→\n   438→The current flat element model (text, image, rect, line, group) needs to evolve toward a **flow-based model** for business documents:\n   439→\n   440→```\n   441→Document\n   442→  Pages[]\n   443→    Page\n   444→      MasterRegions[]        -- header, footer (repeated)\n   445→      ContentRegion          -- main body\n   446→        Blocks[]             -- flow vertically\n   447→          TextBlock          -- rich text with spans\n   448→          Table              -- rows, columns, cells\n   449→          ImageBlock          -- image with caption\n   450→          Spacer             -- explicit vertical space\n   451→          PageBreak          -- force new page\n   452→          RepeatBlock        -- data-bound repeating section\n   453→```\n   454→\n   455→This coexists with the existing **absolute positioning model** for creative documents:\n   456→- Business documents: flow-based, data-bound, multi-page\n   457→- Creative documents: absolute positioning, single-page (or few pages), design-driven\n   458→\n   459→The engine should support both modes, selected per document type.\n   460→\n   461→### Rendering Pipeline\n   462→\n   463→```\n   464→Template (document + merge fields)\n   465→  + Data (JSON from PL/pgSQL)\n   466→  -> Data Binding (resolve {{variables}}, expand repeats, evaluate conditions)\n   467→  -> Layout Engine (compute pages, flow content, break tables)\n   468→  -> Render (SVG for preview, PDF for export)\n   469→```\n   470→\n   471→---\n   472→\n   473→## References\n   474→\n   475→Research based on analysis of:\n   476→- [pdfmake](https://github.com/bpampuch/pdfmake) -- declarative PDF generation in JS\n   477→- [pdfmake documentation](https://pdfmake.github.io/docs/0.1/)\n   478→- [Apache FOP / XSL-FO](https://xmlgraphics.apache.org/fop/) -- complete formatting object specification\n   479→- [XSL-FO Compliance](https://xmlgraphics.apache.org/fop/compliance-static.html)\n   480→- [Typst](https://typst.app/) -- modern typesetting system\n   481→- [Typst automated PDF generation](https://typst.app/blog/2025/automated-generation/)\n   482→- [ReportLab](https://docs.reportlab.com/) -- Python PDF generation\n   483→- [CSS Paged Media Level 3](https://www.w3.org/TR/css-page-3/) -- W3C print specification\n   484→- [Prince XML](https://www.princexml.com/) -- CSS-to-PDF converter\n   485→- [WeasyPrint](https://weasyprint.org/) -- open-source CSS-to-PDF\n   486→- [Factur-X / ZUGFeRD](https://fnfe-mpe.org/factur-x/factur-x_en/) -- hybrid PDF invoice standard\n   487→- [PDF/A specification](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/PDF/A) -- archival PDF standard\n   488→- [Knuth-Plass line-breaking algorithm](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Knuth%E2%80%93Plass_line-breaking_algorithm)\n   489→- [OpenType font features (MDN)](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/CSS/Guides/Fonts/OpenType_fonts)\n   490→- [SVG Filter Effects](https://www.w3.org/TR/SVG11/filters.html)\n   491→- [SVG Gradients and Patterns](https://www.w3.org/TR/SVG11/pservers.html)\n   492→- [French e-invoicing requirements (Stripe)](https://stripe.com/resources/more/mandatory-information-invoice-france)\n   493→- [PDF digital {"parentUuid":"3dcfff08-7197-4277-afa2-5f6b1da51395","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"d6863095-d53e-4d5b-8db9-e2ecc8635efc","agentId":"ae585f19a8c44725e","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_012sLPdmsE42npqwEjkhDamm","type":"tool_result","content":"     1→# ILLUSTRATOR.md — Integration MCP Illustrator\n     2→\n     3→> Moteur de rendu documentaire pour la plateforme pgView.\n     4→> MCP Illustrator est le composant de composition et d'export PDF pour tous les documents : devis, factures, brochures produits, communication.\n     5→\n     6→## Vision\n     7→\n     8→Deux mondes, un seul moteur de rendu :\n     9→\n    10→```\n    11→+------------------------------------------------------------------+\n    12→|  pgView (PostgreSQL)           |  MCP Illustrator                |\n    13→|  ============================  |  ============================== |\n    14→|  Affichage web interactif      |  Documents imprimables (PDF)    |\n    15→|  get_devis() -> HTML browser   |  Composition A4 -> PDF 300 DPI  |\n    16→|  Navigation, CRUD, workflow    |  Brochures, catalogues, com'    |\n    17→|  Temps reel, Alpine.js shell   |  Export pro, bleed, crop marks  |\n    18→+------------------------------------------------------------------+\n    19→                  |                              |\n    20→                  +--------- bridge -------------+\n    21→                  |                              |\n    22→          Donnees metier (PL/pgSQL)     Layout (Illustrator tools)\n    23→```\n    24→\n    25→pgView genere le HTML pour le navigateur. Illustrator compose les documents pour l'impression et l'export. Les donnees viennent du meme endroit : PostgreSQL.\n    26→\n    27→## Pourquoi Illustrator (pas un moteur HTML-to-PDF)\n    28→\n    29→Les moteurs HTML-to-PDF (Gotenberg, WeasyPrint, Puppeteer) convertissent du HTML en PDF. Ca marche, mais :\n    30→\n    31→| | HTML-to-PDF | Illustrator |\n    32→|---|------------|-------------|\n    33→| Controle layout | CSS @page, limites navigateur | Millimetrique, pixel-perfect |\n    34→| Typographie | Approximative (navigateur) | Precise (opentype.js, mesure glyphes) |\n    35→| Images | Contraintes CSS | Crop, zoom, filtres, ombres |\n    36→| Bleed / crop marks | Hack ou impossible | Natif, configurable |\n    37→| Brochures / com' | Hors scope | Use case principal |\n    38→| Template reutilisable | HTML + CSS a maintenir | Document clonable |\n    39→| UI de design | Aucune | Editeur web interactif |\n    40→| Clients potentiels | Aucun (c'est de l'infra) | Produit vendable separement |\n    41→\n    42→L'argument decisif : Illustrator sert **aussi** pour la communication (brochures, flyers, catalogues produit). Un moteur HTML-to-PDF ne fait que de la conversion — Illustrator est un outil de creation.\n    43→\n    44→## Architecture d'integration\n    45→\n    46→### Composants\n    47→\n    48→```\n    49→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\n    50→|  plpgsql-workbench        |        |  mcp-illustrator          |\n    51→|  (MCP server :3100)       |        |  (MCP server, stdio)      |\n    52→|                           |        |                           |\n    53→|  pg_query / pg_get        |        |  doc_new / doc_duplicate  |\n    54→|  -> donnees metier        |        |  batch_add / batch_update |\n    55→|                           |        |  export_pdf / snapshot    |\n    56→|  quote.devis_data(id)     |        |                           |\n    57→|  quote.facture_data(id)   |        |  Templates = documents    |\n    58→|  crm.client_data(id)      |        |  stockes dans SQLite      |\n    59→+---------------------------+        +---------------------------+\n    60→              |                                    |\n    61→              +------------- bridge ---------------+\n    62→              |                                    |\n    63→     +------------------+                          |\n    64→     |  Orchestrateur   |  (agent Claude, MCP tool, ou script)\n    65→     |  1. Query data   |\n    66→     |  2. Clone template|\n    67→     |  3. Fill data     |\n    68→     |  4. Export PDF    |\n    69→     +------------------+\n    70→```\n    71→\n    72→### Flux de generation\n    73→\n    74→```\n    75→1. QUERY     pg_query(\"SELECT quote.devis_data(42)\")\n    76→             -> { numero, date, client, lignes[], totaux, mentions[] }\n    77→\n    78→2. CLONE     doc_duplicate(\"tpl-devis-standard\")\n    79→             -> nouveau document \"DEV-2026-042\"\n    80→\n    81→3. FILL      batch_update([\n    82→               { name: \"numero\",     text: \"DEV-2026-042\" },\n    83→               { name: \"date\",       text: \"13 mars 2026\" },\n    84→               { name: \"client-nom\", text: \"Dupont SARL\" },\n    85→               ...\n    86→             ])\n    87→             + generation dynamique du tableau de lignes\n    88→\n    89→4. EXPORT    export_pdf({ format: \"A4\", home_print: true })\n    90→             -> PDF binaire\n    91→\n    92→5. CLEANUP   doc_delete(\"DEV-2026-042\")\n    93→             (ou archivage si besoin de re-generation)\n    94→```\n    95→\n    96→## Templates\n    97→\n    98→### Principe : template = document\n    99→\n   100→Pas de DSL, pas de Jinja, pas de moteur de substitution. Un template est un **document Illustrator standard** avec des elements nommes :\n   101→\n   102→```\n   103→tpl-devis-standard (A4 portrait)\n   104→├── logo              image    (x:15, y:15, w:40, h:20)\n   105→├── entreprise-nom    text     (x:15, y:40, \"ACME SARL\")\n   106→├── entreprise-addr   text     (x:15, y:48, \"12 rue des Lilas...\")\n   107→├── entreprise-siret  text     (x:15, y:62, \"SIRET: 123 456 789 00001\")\n   108→├── entreprise-tva    text     (x:15, y:67, \"TVA: FR12345678900\")\n   109→├── client-nom        text     (x:120, y:40, \"[client]\")\n   110→├── client-addr       text     (x:120, y:48, \"[adresse]\")\n   111→├── titre             text     (x:15, y:90, \"DEVIS DEV-XXXX-XXX\")\n   112→├── date              text     (x:160, y:90, \"[date]\")\n   113→├── validite          text     (x:160, y:96, \"Valide 30 jours\")\n   114→├── table-header      group    (y:110)\n   115→│   ├── col-desc      text     \"Description\"\n   116→│   ├── col-qte       text     \"Qte\"\n   117→│   ├── col-unite     text     \"Unite\"\n   118→│   ├── col-pu        text     \"P.U. HT\"\n   119→│   ├── col-tva       text     \"TVA\"\n   120→│   └── col-total     text     \"Total HT\"\n   121→├── table-lines       group    (y:118, genere dynamiquement)\n   122→├── total-ht          text     (x:160, y: calc, \"Total HT: 1 234,00\")\n   123→├── total-tva         text     (x:160, y: calc, \"TVA 20%:   246,80\")\n   124→├── total-ttc         text     (x:160, y: calc, \"Total TTC: 1 480,80\")\n   125→├── mentions          group    (y: bottom - 40)\n   126→│   ├── mention-1     text     \"Delai de paiement: 30 jours...\"\n   127→│   ├── mention-2     text     \"Penalites de retard: 10%...\"\n   128→│   └── mention-3     text     \"Indemnite forfaitaire: 40 EUR\"\n   129→├── watermark         text     (center, rotate:-45, opacity:0.08, \"BROUILLON\")\n   130→└── footer            group    (y: bottom - 10)\n   131→    ├── page-num      text     \"Page 1/1\"\n   132→    └── generation    text     \"Genere le 13/03/2026\"\n   133→```\n   134→\n   135→### Convention de nommage\n   136→\n   137→Les elements portent des noms semantiques que l'orchestrateur connait :\n   138→\n   139→| Prefixe | Contenu | Source |\n   140→|---------|---------|--------|\n   141→| `entreprise-*` | Coordonnees emetteur | `workbench.config('quote', ...)` |\n   142→| `client-*` | Coordonnees destinataire | `crm.client` |\n   143→| `titre`, `numero`, `date` | En-tete document | `quote.devis` / `quote.facture` |\n   144→| `table-header`, `table-lines` | Tableau des lignes | `quote.ligne` |\n   145→| `total-*` | Bloc totaux | Calcul `_total_ht/tva/ttc` |\n   146→| `mention-*` | Mentions legales | `quote.mention` |\n   147→| `watermark` | Filigrane conditionnel | Statut (BROUILLON, PAYE, ANNULE) |\n   148→| `footer` | Pied de page | Metadata generation |\n   149→\n   150→### Types de templates\n   151→\n   152→| Template | Format | Usage |\n   153→|----------|--------|-------|\n   154→| `tpl-devis-standard` | A4 portrait | Devis classique |\n   155→| `tpl-facture-standard` | A4 portrait | Facture |\n   156→| `tpl-bon-livraison` | A4 portrait | Bon de livraison |\n   157→| `tpl-avoir` | A4 portrait | Avoir / credit |\n   158→| `tpl-relance` | A4 portrait | Lettre de relance |\n   159→| `tpl-brochure-produit` | A4 paysage | Fiche produit catalogue |\n   160→| `tpl-catalogue-*` | A3/A4 | Catalogue multi-pages |\n   161→\n   162→### Personnalisation par tenant\n   163→\n   164→Les templates sont des documents Illustrator. Personnaliser = modifier le document :\n   165→\n   166→1. **Branding** — Remplacer le logo, les couleurs, les polices\n   167→2. **Layout** — Deplacer les blocs, redimensionner\n   168→3. **Contenu fixe** — Modifier les mentions, ajouter un slogan\n   169→4. **Nouveau template** — Dupliquer + modifier via l'UI web (localhost:3333)\n   170→\n   171→Pas de systeme de \"theme\" abstrait. Le template EST le design final — l'utilisateur ou l'agent le modifie directement.\n   172→\n   173→## Donnees metier\n   174→\n   175→### Fonctions d'extraction\n   176→\n   177→Chaque module expose une fonction `*_data()` qui retourne un JSONB structure, pret pour le remplissage :\n   178→\n   179→```sql\n   180→-- quote.devis_data(p_id int) RETURNS jsonb\n   181→{\n   182→  \"numero\": \"DEV-2026-042\",\n   183→  \"date\": \"2026-03-13\",\n   184→  \"validite\": \"2026-04-12\",\n   185→  \"statut\": \"brouillon\",\n   186→\n   187→  \"entreprise\": {\n   188→    \"nom\": \"ACME SARL\",\n   189→    \"adresse\": \"12 rue des Lilas, 39000 Lons-le-Saunier\",\n   190→    \"siret\": \"123 456 789 00001\",\n   191→    \"tva_intra\": \"FR12345678900\",\n   192→    \"telephone\": \"03 84 XX XX XX\",\n   193→    \"email\": \"contact@acme.fr\"\n   194→  },\n   195→\n   196→  \"client\": {\n   197→    \"nom\": \"Dupont SARL\",\n   198→    \"adresse\": \"5 avenue de la Gare, 25000 Besancon\",\n   199→    \"siret\": \"987 654 321 00001\"\n   200→  },"}]},"uuid":"41a11c3e-c227-4eb4-a89b-1e1bf68a3c40","timestamp":"2026-03-13T22:38:16.547Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"3dcfff08-7197-4277-afa2-5f6b1da51395","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/alexandreboyer/dev/projects/plpgsql-workbench","sessionId":"32666746-590f-450a-9377-59546bb90632","version":"2.1.75","gitBranch":"main","slug":"quizzical-honking-yao"}

10→import { resolveImagePath, loadImageAsDataUri, getImageDimensions } from \"./images.js\";\n    11→import {\n    12→  getActiveDoc,\n    13→  getDocuments,\n    14→  getActiveDocName,\n    15→  setActiveDoc,\n    16→  getSelectedElementId,\n    17→  getSelectedAsset,\n    18→  genId,\n    19→  saveDocToDisk,\n    20→  getStore,\n    21→  getDocList,\n    22→  listAssets,\n    23→  deleteDocument,\n    24→  markDirty,\n    25→} from \"./documents.js\";\n    26→import { bus } from \"./bus.js\";\n    27→import { buildSVG } from \"./svg.js\";\n    28→import { checkLayout } from \"./layout.js\";\n    29→import { measureTextWidth, wrapText } from \"./fonts.js\";\n    30→import { resolvePosition, hasRelativeArgs, computeAlign, computeDistribute } from \"./positioning.js\";\n    31→import { generatePdf } from \"./pdf.js\";\n    32→import { requestFromClient } from \"./ws-bridge.js\";\n    33→import type { Element, GroupElement, Document } from \"./types.js\";\n    34→import { findInTree, findInTreeWithParent, countElements, reassignIds, insertIntoGroup, isAncestorOf } from \"./tree.js\";\n    35→\n    36→function txt(t: string) {\n    37→  return { content: [{ type: \"text\" as const, text: t }] };\n    38→}\n    39→\n    40→/** Resolve element by ID or name (recursive) */\n    41→function findEl(doc: Document, idOrName: string): Element | undefined {\n    42→  return findInTree(doc.elements, idOrName);\n    43→}\n    44→\n    45→/** Recursively apply offset to element (handles groups) */\n    46→function applyOffset(el: Element, dx: number, dy: number): void {\n    47→  if (el.type === \"group\") {\n    48→    for (const child of (el as GroupElement).children) applyOffset(child, dx, dy);\n    49→    return;\n    50→  }\n    51→  if (el.type === \"line\") {\n    52→    (el as any).x1 += dx; (el as any).y1 += dy;\n    53→    (el as any).x2 += dx; (el as any).y2 += dy;\n    54→  } else {\n    55→    (el as any).x += dx;\n    56→    (el as any).y += dy;\n    57→  }\n    58→}\n    59→\n    60→/** Recursively sanitize elements for JSON output (hide href) */\n    61→function sanitizeElements(elements: Element[]): any[] {\n    62→  return elements.map((el) => {\n    63→    if (el.type === \"image\") {\n    64→      const { href, ...rest } = el;\n    65→      return { ...rest, href: \"(base64)\" };\n    66→    }\n    67→    if (el.type === \"group\") {\n    68→      return { ...el, children: sanitizeElements((el as GroupElement).children) };\n    69→    }\n    70→    return el;\n    71→  });\n    72→}\n    73→\n    74→/** Compact text representation of document state */\n    75→function compactState(d: Document): string {\n    76→  const stars = d.meta?.rating ? \"★\".repeat(d.meta.rating) + \"☆\".repeat(5 - d.meta.rating) : \"\";\n    77→  const meta = [\n    78→    stars,\n    79→    d.meta?.designNotes ? `design:${d.meta.designNotes.length}c` : \"\",\n    80→    d.meta?.teamNotes ? `team:${d.meta.teamNotes.length}c` : \"\",\n    81→  ].filter(Boolean).join(\"  \");\n    82→\n    83→  const total = countElements(d.elements);\n    84→  const header = `Document: \"${d.name}\" [${d.category}]  ${d.canvas.format} ${d.canvas.orientation} ${d.canvas.w}×${d.canvas.h} bg:${d.canvas.bg}  |  ${total} elements`;\n    85→  const metaLine = meta ? `Meta: ${meta}` : \"\";\n    86→  const selId = getSelectedElementId();\n    87→  const selLine = selId ? `Selected: ${selId}` : \"\";\n    88→\n    89→  const lines: string[] = [header];\n    90→  if (metaLine) lines.push(metaLine);\n    91→  if (selLine) lines.push(selLine);\n    92→  lines.push(\"─\".repeat(60));\n    93→\n    94→  function renderEl(el: Element, indent: number): void {\n    95→    const pad = \"  \".repeat(indent);\n    96→    const nameTag = el.name ? ` (${el.name})` : \"\";\n    97→    const id = el.id + nameTag;\n    98→    let info: string;\n    99→\n   100→    switch (el.type) {\n   101→      case \"group\": {\n   102→        const g = el as GroupElement;\n   103→        info = `group  [${g.children.length} children]`;\n   104→        if (el.opacity < 1) info += ` op:${el.opacity}`;\n   105→        if (el.rotation) info += ` rot:${el.rotation}`;\n   106→        lines.push(`${pad}${id.padEnd(Math.max(1, 20 - indent * 2))} ${info}`);\n   107→        for (const child of g.children) renderEl(child, indent + 1);\n   108→        return;\n   109→      }\n   110→      case \"text\": {\n   111→        const preview = el.text.length > 25 ? el.text.slice(0, 24) + \"…\" : el.text;\n   112→        const props = [`sz:${el.fontSize}`, el.textAnchor !== \"start\" ? el.textAnchor.slice(0, 3) : \"\", `fill:${el.fill}`];\n   113→        if (el.maxWidth) props.push(`mw:${el.maxWidth}`);\n   114→        info = `text   \"${preview}\"  x:${r(el.x)} y:${r(el.y)}  ${props.filter(Boolean).join(\" \")}`;\n   115→        break;\n   116→      }\n   117→      case \"image\": {\n   118→        const fname = el.path || \"?\";\n   119→        info = `image  ${fname}  x:${r(el.x)} y:${r(el.y)}  ${r(el.width)}×${r(el.height)}`;\n   120→        if (el.opacity < 1) info += ` op:${el.opacity}`;\n   121→        break;\n   122→      }\n   123→      case \"rect\":\n   124→        info = `rect   x:${r(el.x)} y:${r(el.y)}  ${r(el.width)}×${r(el.height)}  fill:${el.fill}`;\n   125→        if (el.stroke !== \"none\") info += ` stroke:${el.stroke}`;\n   126→        break;\n   127→      case \"line\":\n   128→        info = `line   ${r(el.x1)},${r(el.y1)}→${r(el.x2)},${r(el.y2)}  stroke:${el.stroke} w:${el.strokeWidth}`;\n   129→        break;\n   130→      default:\n   131→        info = `${el.type}`;\n   132→    }\n   133→\n   134→    if (el.opacity < 1 && el.type !== \"image\") info += ` op:${el.opacity}`;\n   135→    if (el.rotation) info += ` rot:${el.rotation}`;\n   136→\n   137→    lines.push(`${pad}${id.padEnd(Math.max(1, 20 - indent * 2))} ${info}`);\n   138→  }\n   139→\n   140→  for (const el of d.elements) renderEl(el, 0);\n   141→\n   142→  return lines.join(\"\\n\");\n   143→}\n   144→\n   145→function r(v: number): number { return Math.round(v * 10) / 10; }\n   146→\n   147→export async function handleTool(name: string, args: any) {\n   148→  switch (name) {\n   149→    // ---- Documents ----\n   150→    case \"doc_new\": {\n   151→      const fmt = args.format || \"A3\";\n   152→      const f = FORMATS[fmt] || FORMATS.A3;\n   153→      const orient = args.orientation || \"portrait\";\n   154→      const isL = orient === \"paysage\" && !SCREEN_FORMATS.has(fmt);\n   155→      const w = isL ? f.h : f.w, h = isL ? f.w : f.h;\n   156→      const newDoc = {\n   157→        name: args.name,\n   158→        category: args.category || \"general\",\n   159→        canvas: { format: fmt, orientation: orient, w, h, bg: args.background || \"#ffffff\" },\n   160→        meta: {},\n   161→        elements: [] as any[],\n   162→        nextId: 1,\n   163→      };\n   164→      getDocuments().set(args.name, newDoc);\n   165→      setActiveDoc(args.name);\n   166→      bus.emit(\"document:created\", { name: args.name });\n   167→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `Nouveau document \"${args.name}\" (${fmt} ${orient})`, level: \"success\" });\n   168→      return txt(`New doc \"${args.name}\" [${newDoc.category}] (${fmt} ${orient} ${w}x${h}mm)`);\n   169→    }\n   170→\n   171→    case \"doc_save\": {\n   172→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   173→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   174→      if (args.name && args.name !== d.name) {\n   175→        d.name = args.name;\n   176→        getDocuments().delete(getActiveDocName()!);\n   177→        getDocuments().set(args.name, d);\n   178→        setActiveDoc(args.name);\n   179→      }\n   180→      saveDocToDisk(d);\n   181→      bus.emit(\"document:saved\", { name: d.name });\n   182→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `Document \"${d.name}\" sauvegardé`, level: \"success\" });\n   183→      return txt(`Saved \"${d.name}\" → DB`);\n   184→    }\n   185→\n   186→    case \"doc_load\": {\n   187→      const documents = getDocuments();\n   188→      if (!documents.has(args.name)) {\n   189→        const doc = getStore().loadOne(args.name);\n   190→        if (!doc) return txt(`Document \"${args.name}\" not found`);\n   191→        documents.set(doc.name, doc);\n   192→      }\n   193→      setActiveDoc(args.name);\n   194→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   195→      bus.emit(\"document:loaded\", { name: args.name });\n   196→      return txt(`Loaded \"${d!.name}\" (${d!.canvas.format}, ${countElements(d!.elements)} elements)`);\n   197→    }\n   198→\n   199→    case \"doc_list\": {\n   200→      const list = getDocList();\n   201→      if (!list.length) return txt(\"No documents.\");\n   202→      const lines = list.map(\n   203→        (d) => `- ${d.name} [${d.category}] (${d.format}, ${d.count} elements)`\n   204→      );\n   205→      return txt(lines.join(\"\\n\"));\n   206→    }\n   207→\n   208→    case \"doc_delete\": {\n   209→      const documents = getDocuments();\n   210→      if (!documents.has(args.name)) return txt(`Document \"${args.name}\" not found`);\n   211→      if (documents.size <= 1) return txt(`Cannot delete the only document`);\n   212→      const wasActive = getActiveDocName() === args.name;\n   213→      deleteDocument(args.name);\n   214→      bus.emit(\"document:deleted\", { name: args.name });\n   215→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `Document \"${args.name}\" supprimé`, level: \"info\" });\n   216→      if (wasActive) bus.emit(\"document:loaded\", { name: getActiveDocName() });\n   217→      return txt(`Deleted \"${args.name}\"${wasActive ? ` → switched to \"${getActiveDocName()}\"` : \"\"}`);\n   218→    }\n   219→\n   220→    case \"doc_duplicate\": {\n   221→      const sourceName = args.source || getActiveDocName();\n   222→      if (!sourceName) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   223→      const sourceDoc = getDocuments().get(sourceName);\n   224→      if (!sourceDoc) return txt(`Document \"${sourceName}\" not found`);\n   225→      if (getDocuments().has(args.name)) return txt(`Document \"${args.name}\" already exists`);\n   226→      const clone = structuredClone(sourceDoc);\n   227→      clone.name = args.name;\n   228→      // Reassign element IDs (recursive for groups)\n   229→      clone.nextId = reassignIds(clone.elements, 1);\n   230→      getDocuments().set(clone.name, clone);\n   231→      setActiveDoc(clone.name);\n   232→      saveDocToDisk(clone);\n   233→      bus.emit(\"document:created\", { name: clone.name });\n   234→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `Document \"${sourceName}\" cloné → \"${clone.name}\"`, level: \"success\" });\n   235→      return txt(`Cloned \"${sourceName}\" → \"${clone.name}\" (${clone.elements.length} elements)`);\n   236→    }\n   237→\n   238→    case \"doc_rename\": {\n   239→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   240→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   241→      if (getDocuments().has(args.name)) return txt(`Document \"${args.name}\" already exists`);\n   242→      const oldName = d.name;\n   243→      getStore().deleteDoc(oldName);\n   244→      getDocuments().delete(oldName);\n   245→      d.name = args.name;\n   246→      getDocuments().set(args.name, d);\n   247→      setActiveDoc(args.name);\n   248→      saveDocToDisk(d);\n   249→      bus.emit(\"document:loaded\", { name: args.name });\n   250→      bus.emit(\"toast\", { text: `\"${oldName}\" → \"${args.name}\"`, level: \"success\" });\n   251→      return txt(`Renamed \"${oldName}\" → \"${args.name}\"`);\n   252→    }\n   253→\n   254→    case \"element_duplicate\": {\n   255→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   256→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   257→      const el = findEl(d, args.id_or_name);\n   258→      if (!el) return txt(`Element \"${args.id_or_name}\" not found`);\n   259→      const clone = structuredClone(el);\n   260→      // Reassign IDs recursively for groups\n   261→      if (clone.type === \"group\") {\n   262→        clone.id = `e${d.nextId++}`;\n   263→        d.nextId = reassignIds((clone as GroupElement).children, d.nextId);\n   264→      } else {\n   265→        clone.id = `e${d.nextId++}`;\n   266→      }\n   267→      delete clone.name;\n   268→      delete (clone as any).href;\n   269→      const dx = args.offset_x ?? 5;\n   270→      const dy = args.offset_y ?? 5;\n   271→      applyOffset(clone, dx, dy);\n   272→      d.elements.push(clone);\n   273→      markDirty();\n   274→      bus.emit(\"element:added\", { id: clone.id });\n   275→      return txt(`Duplicated \"${args.id_or_name}\" → ${clone.id} (offset +${dx},+${dy}mm)`);\n   276→    }\n   277→\n   278→    // ---- Assets ----\n   279→    case \"list_assets\": {\n   280→      const files = listAssets();\n   281→      if (!files.length) return txt(`No images in ${relative(PROJECT_ROOT, ASSETS_DIR)}/`);\n   282→      return txt(`Assets (${ASSETS_DIR}):\\n${files.map((f) => `- ${f}`).join(\"\\n\")}`);\n   283→    }\n   284→\n   285→    // ---- Canvas ----\n   286→    case \"canvas_setup\": {\n   287→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   288→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   289→      const fmt = args.format || d.canvas.format;\n   290→      const f = FORMATS[fmt] || FORMATS.A3;\n   291→      const orient = args.orientation || d.canvas.orientation || \"portrait\";\n   292→      const isL = orient === \"paysage\" && !SCREEN_FORMATS.has(fmt);\n   293→      const w = isL ? f.h : f.w, h = isL ? f.w : f.h;\n   294→      d.canvas = {\n   295→        format: fmt,\n   296→        orientation: orient,\n   297→        w, h,\n   298→        bg: args.background || d.canvas.bg,\n   299→      };\n   300→      bus.emit(\"canvas:changed\", {});\n   301→      return txt(`Canvas: ${fmt} ${orient} (${w}x${h}mm) bg=${d.canvas.bg}`);\n   302→    }\n   303→\n   304→    // ---- Elements ----\n   305→    case \"add_text\": {\n   306→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   307→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   308→      // Resolve relative positioning\n   309→      let x = args.x, y = args.y;\n   310→      if (hasRelativeArgs(args)) {\n   311→        try {\n   312→          const pos = resolvePosition(d, \"text\", args);\n   313→          if (pos.x != null) x = pos.x;\n   314→          if (pos.y != null) y = pos.y;\n   315→        } catch (e: any) {\n   316→          return txt(`Position error: ${e.message}`);\n   317→        }\n   318→      }\n   319→      if (x == null || y == null) return txt(\"Missing coordinates: provide x/y or use relative positioning (below/above/right_of/left_of/center_h/center_v)\");\n   320→      const eid = genId();\n   321→      const newEl = {\n   322→        id: eid,\n   323→        name: args.name || undefined,\n   324→        type: \"text\",\n   325→        x, y,\n   326→        text: args.text,\n   327→        fontSize: args.fontSize ?? 8,\n   328→        fontFamily: args.fontFamily ?? \"Libre Baskerville\",\n   329→        fontWeight: args.fontWeight ?? \"bold\",\n   330→        fontStyle: args.fontStyle ?? \"normal\",\n   331→        fill: args.fill ?? \"#1C1C1C\",\n   332→        textAnchor: args.textAnchor ?? \"start\",\n   333→        maxWidth: args.maxWidth ?? null,\n   334→        opacity: args.opacity ?? 1,\n   335→        rotation: args.rotation ?? 0,\n   336→      } as any;\n   337→      if (!insertIntoGroup(d.elements, newEl, args.group)) return txt(`Group \"${args.group}\" not found`);\n   338→      bus.emit(\"element:added\", { id: eid });\n   339→      return txt(`Text \"${args.text.slice(0, 40)}\" → ${eid}${args.name ? ` (${args.name})` : \"\"}`);\n   340→    }\n   341→\n   342→    case \"add_image\": {\n   343→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   344→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   345→      const absPath = resolveImagePath(args.path);\n   346→      if (!absPath || !existsSync(absPath))\n   347→        return txt(`Image not found: ${args.path} (looked in ${ASSETS_DIR})`);\n   348→      const href = loadImageAsDataUri(args.path);\n   349→      // Resolve relative positioning\n   350→      let x = args.x, y = args.y;\n   351→      if (hasRelativeArgs(args)) {\n   352→        try {\n   353→          const pos = resolvePosition(d, \"image\", args);\n   354→          if (pos.x != null) x = pos.x;\n   355→          if (pos.y != null) y = pos.y;\n   356→        } catch (e: any) {\n   357→          return txt(`Position error: ${e.message}`);\n   358→        }\n   359→      }\n   360→      if (x == null || y == null) return txt(\"Missing coordinates: provide x/y or use relative positioning (below/above/right_of/left_of/center_h/center_v)\");\n   361→      const eid = genId();\n   362→      const dims = getImageDimensions(args.path);\n   363→      const newEl = {\n   364→        id: eid,\n   365→        name: args.name || undefined,\n   366→        type: \"image\",\n   367→        x, y,\n   368→        width: args.width,\n   369→        height: args.height,\n   370→        path: args.path,\n   371→        href,\n   372→        preserveAspectRatio: args.preserveAspectRatio ?? \"xMidYMid slice\",\n   373→        naturalWidth: dims?.w ?? args.width,\n   374→        naturalHeight: dims?.h ?? args.height,\n   375→        objectFit: args.objectFit ?? \"cover\",\n   376→        cropX: args.cropX ?? 0.5,\n   377→        cropY: args.cropY ?? 0.5,\n   378→        cropZoom: args.cropZoom ?? 1,\n   379→        flipH: args.flipH ?? false,\n   380→        flipV: args.flipV ?? false,\n   381→        opacity: args.opacity ?? 1,\n   382→        rotation: args.rotation ?? 0,\n   383→        brightness: args.brightness ?? 100,\n   384→        contrast: args.contrast ?? 100,\n   385→        grayscale: args.grayscale ?? 0,\n   386→        borderWidth: args.borderWidth ?? 0,\n   387→        borderColor: args.borderColor ?? \"#000000\",\n   388→        borderRadius: args.borderRadius ?? 0,\n   389→        shadowX: args.shadowX ?? 0,\n   390→        shadowY: args.shadowY ?? 0,\n   391→        shadowBlur: args.shadowBlur ?? 0,\n   392→        shadowColor: args.shadowColor ?? \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\",\n   393→      } as any;\n   394→      if (!insertIntoGroup(d.elements, newEl, args.group)) return txt(`Group \"${args.group}\" not found`);\n   395→      bus.emit(\"element:added\", { id: eid });\n   396→      return txt(`Image \"${basename(args.path)}\" → ${eid}${args.name ? ` (${args.name})` : \"\"}`);\n   397→    }\n   398→\n   399→    case \"add_rect\": {\n   400→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   401→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   402→      // Resolve relative positioning\n   403→      let x = args.x, y = args.y;\n   404→      if (hasRelativeArgs(args)) {\n   405→        try {\n   406→          const pos = resolvePosition(d, \"rect\", args);\n   407→          if (pos.x != null) x = pos.x;\n   408→          if (pos.y != null) y = pos.y;\n   409→        } catch (e: any) {\n   410→          return txt(`Position error: ${e.message}`);\n   411→        }\n   412→      }\n   413→      if (x == null || y == null) return txt(\"Missing coordinates: provide x/y or use relative positioning (below/above/right_of/left_of/center_h/center_v)\");\n   414→      const eid = genId();\n   415→      const newEl = {\n   416→        id: eid,\n   417→        name: args.name || undefined,\n   418→        type: \"rect\",\n   419→        x, y,\n   420→        width: args.width,\n   421→        height: args.height,\n   422→        fill: args.fill ?? \"#000000\",\n   423→        stroke: args.stroke ?? } as any;\n   429→      if (!insertIntoGroup(d.elements, newEl, args.group)) return txt(`Group \"${args.group}\" not found`);\n   430→      bus.emit(\"element:added\", { id: eid });\n   431→      return txt(`Rect → ${eid}${args.name ? ` (${args.name})` : \"\"}`);\n   432→    }\n   433→\n   434→    case \"add_line\": {\n   435→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   436→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   437→      // Resolve relative positioning\n   438→      let x1 = args.x1, y1 = args.y1, x2 = args.x2, y2 = args.y2;\n   439→      if (hasRelativeArgs(args)) {\n   440→        try {\n   441→          const pos = resolvePosition(d, \"line\", args);\n   442→          if (pos.x1 != null) x1 = pos.x1;\n   443→          if (pos.y1 != null) y1 = pos.y1;\n   444→          if (pos.x2 != null) x2 = pos.x2;\n   445→          if (pos.y2 != null) y2 = pos.y2;\n   446→        } catch (e: any) {\n   447→          return txt(`Position error: ${e.message}`);\n   448→        }\n   449→      }\n   450→      const eid = genId();\n   451→      const newEl = {\n   452→        id: eid,\n   453→        name: args.name || undefined,\n   454→        type: \"line\",\n   455→        x1, y1, x2, y2,\n   456→        stroke: args.stroke ?? \"#000000\",\n   457→        strokeWidth: args.strokeWidth ?? 0.5,\n   458→        opacity: args.opacity ?? 1,\n   459→        rotation: args.rotation ?? 0,\n   460→      } as any;\n   461→      if (!insertIntoGroup(d.elements, newEl, args.group)) return txt(`Group \"${args.group}\" not found`);\n   462→      bus.emit(\"element:added\", { id: eid });\n   463→      return txt(`Line → ${eid}${args.name ? ` (${args.name})` : \"\"}`);\n   464→    }\n   465→\n   466→    case \"update_element\": {\n   467→      const d = getActiveDoc();\n   468→      if (!d) return txt(\"No active document\");\n   469→      const el = findEl(d, args.id);\n   470→      if (!el) return txt(`Not found: ${args.id}`);\n   471→      if (args.props.path && el.type === \"image\") {\n   472→        args.props.href = loadImageAsDataUri(args.props.path);\n   473→        const dims = getImageDimensions(args.props.path);\n   474→
