The ILLUSTRATOR-PRIMITIVES.md and ILLUSTRATOR-GRAPHICS.md files are JSONL conversation logs, not markdown. I've read the actual source from `mcp-illustrator/src/types.ts`, `svg.ts`, and `handlers.ts`. Let me now produce the complete visual effects spec.\n\n---\n\n# Visual Effects System Specification for `document.render_svg`\n\nThis document is the authoritative spec for all visual effects applied to `document.element` primitives. It covers props storage in JSONB, SVG rendering output, applicability, composability, and implementation priority.\n\n**Reference baseline**: The existing mcp-illustrator implements effects only on the `image` type. This spec extends and generalizes effects across all primitive types.\n\n---\n\n## 0. Foundation: Element Type Set\n\nThe engine stores 7 primitive types in `document.element`. All effects in this spec reference this set by short names:\n\n| Short name | Type | Notes |\n|---|---|---|\n| `text` | Text element | Has fill (= text color), no geometric fill |\n| `rect` | Rectangle | Has fill + stroke natively |\n| `line` | Line segment (x1,y1 -> x2,y2) | No fill, stroke only |\n| `circle` | Circle | Has fill + stroke |\n| `ellipse` | Ellipse | Has fill + stroke |\n| `image` | Raster image | No fill (image content is the fill) |\n| `path` | SVG path data | Has fill + stroke |\n| `group` | Container | Effects on group apply to all children via `<g>` |\n\n\"Fill-capable\" = rect, circle, ellipse, path, text (as text color)\n\"Stroke-capable\" = rect, line, circle, ellipse, path, text (as outline), image (border is a separate overlay — see section 7)\n\"Filter-capable\" = all types\n\"Shadow-capable\" = all types\n\"Clip-capable\" = image, rect, circle, ellipse, group\n\n---\n\n## 1. Fill Effects\n\n### 1.1 Solid Color Fill\n\n**Applies to**: rect, circle, ellipse, path, text (as text color)\n**Does not apply to**: line, image (image content fills the frame)\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"fill\": \"#3b82f6\"\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range / Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `fill` | string | `\"#000000\"` for text, `\"none\"` for shapes without explicit fill | hex `#rrggbb`, `#rgb`, `rgba(r,g,b,a)`, `\"none\"`, `\"transparent\"` |\n\n**SVG output**:\n```xml\n<rect ... fill=\"#3b82f6\"/>\n<text ... fill=\"#3b82f6\">...</text>\n<circle ... fill=\"none\"/>\n```\n\nNo `<defs>` entry required. Solid fill is a direct attribute.\n\nPriority: MUST (Phase 1) — already implemented for rect and text in baseline.\n\n---\n\n### 1.2 Linear Gradient Fill\n\n**Applies to**: rect, circle, ellipse, path, text\n**Does not apply to**: line, image\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"fill\": \"linear-gradient\",\n  \"gradient\": {\n    \"type\": \"linear\",\n    \"angle\": 90,\n    \"stops\": [\n      { \"offset\": 0, \"color\": \"#3b82f6\", \"opacity\": 1 },\n      { \"offset\": 1, \"color\": \"#1e40af\", \"opacity\": 1 }\n    ]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range / Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `fill` | string | — | literal `\"linear-gradient\"` signals gradient mode |\n| `gradient.type` | string | — | `\"linear\"` |\n| `gradient.angle` | number | `90` | degrees, 0=bottom-to-top, 90=left-to-right, 180=top-to-bottom, 270=right-to-left |\n| `gradient.stops` | array | — | min 2 stops |\n| `gradient.stops[].offset` | number | — | 0.0 to 1.0 |\n| `gradient.stops[].color` | string | — | hex or rgba |\n| `gradient.stops[].opacity` | number | `1` | 0.0 to 1.0 |\n\n**SVG output** (renderer generates unique `id` per element):\n```xml\n<defs>\n  <linearGradient id=\"lg_e7\" x1=\"0%\" y1=\"0%\" x2=\"100%\" y2=\"0%\"\n                  gradientUnits=\"userSpaceOnUse\"\n                  gradientTransform=\"rotate(90, cx, cy)\">\n    <stop offset=\"0%\" stop-color=\"#3b82f6\" stop-opacity=\"1\"/>\n    <stop offset=\"100%\" stop-color=\"#1e40af\" stop-opacity=\"1\"/>\n  </linearGradient>\n</defs>\n<rect ... fill=\"url(#lg_e7)\"/>\n```\n\nAngle-to-SVG coordinates: convert `angle` to `(x1,y1,x2,y2)` using unit vector on element bounding box center. For `gradientUnits=\"objectBoundingBox\"` (simpler): `x1=\"0.5\" y1=\"1\" x2=\"0.5\" y2=\"0\"` for 0 degrees, rotate via `gradientTransform`. Using `userSpaceOnUse` with element cx/cy gives pixel-perfect results.\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2)\n\n---\n\n### 1.3 Radial Gradient Fill\n\n**Applies to**: rect, circle, ellipse, path, text\n**Does not apply to**: line, image\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"fill\": \"radial-gradient\",\n  \"gradient\": {\n    \"type\": \"radial\",\n    \"cx\": 0.5,\n    \"cy\": 0.5,\n    \"r\": 0.5,\n    \"stops\": [\n      { \"offset\": 0, \"color\": \"#ffffff\", \"opacity\": 1 },\n      { \"offset\": 1, \"color\": \"#3b82f6\", \"opacity\": 0 }\n    ]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range / Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `gradient.cx` | number | `0.5` | 0.0 to 1.0 — center X relative to bounding box |\n| `gradient.cy` | number | `0.5` | 0.0 to 1.0 — center Y relative to bounding box |\n| `gradient.r` | number | `0.5` | 0.0 to 1.0 — radius relative to bounding box |\n\n**SVG output**:\n```xml\n<defs>\n  <radialGradient id=\"rg_e7\" cx=\"50%\" cy=\"50%\" r=\"50%\"\n                  gradientUnits=\"objectBoundingBox\">\n    <stop offset=\"0%\" stop-color=\"#ffffff\" stop-opacity=\"1\"/>\n    <stop offset=\"100%\" stop-color=\"#3b82f6\" stop-opacity=\"0\"/>\n  </radialGradient>\n</defs>\n<rect ... fill=\"url(#rg_e7)\"/>\n```\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n### 1.4 No Fill / Transparent\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{ \"fill\": \"none\" }\n```\n\n**SVG output**: `fill=\"none\"` directly on element. No defs.\n\nPriority: MUST (Phase 1) — needed for outline-only rects.\n\n---\n\n### 1.5 Pattern Fill (Hatching, Dots)\n\nFuture. Phase 3 only.\n\n**Props JSONB sketch** (not final):\n```json\n{\n  \"fill\": \"pattern\",\n  \"pattern\": {\n    \"type\": \"hatch\",\n    \"angle\": 45,\n    \"spacing\": 3,\n    \"strokeColor\": \"#333333\",\n    \"strokeWidth\": 0.5\n  }\n}\n```\n\nUses SVG `<pattern>` in `<defs>`. Not specified further in this version.\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n## 2. Stroke Effects\n\n### 2.1 Solid Stroke\n\n**Applies to**: rect, line, circle, ellipse, path, text (outline effect), group\n**Does not apply to**: image (image uses `borderWidth`/`borderColor` overlay — section 7)\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"stroke\": \"#000000\",\n  \"strokeWidth\": 0.5\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range / Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `stroke` | string | `\"none\"` | hex, rgba, `\"none\"` |\n| `strokeWidth` | number | `0` | mm. 0 = no stroke even if stroke color set |\n\n**SVG output**:\n```xml\n<rect ... stroke=\"#000000\" stroke-width=\"0.5\"/>\n<line ... stroke=\"#000000\" stroke-width=\"0.5\"/>\n```\n\nPriority: MUST (Phase 1) — already in baseline for rect and line.\n\n---\n\n### 2.2 Dashed / Dotted Stroke\n\n**Applies to**: same as 2.1\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"stroke\": \"#000000\",\n  \"strokeWidth\": 0.5,\n  \"strokeDash\": \"dashed\"\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `strokeDash` | string | `\"solid\"` | `\"solid\"`, `\"dashed\"`, `\"dotted\"`, `\"dash-dot\"`, `\"custom\"` |\n| `strokeDasharray` | string | `null` | SVG dasharray string — only used when `strokeDash = \"custom\"` |\n\n**Preset-to-dasharray mapping** (in mm, scaled by strokeWidth):\n\n| Preset | SVG dasharray (relative to strokeWidth × factor) |\n|---|---|\n| `solid` | (no attribute) |\n| `dashed` | `\"5,3\"` |\n| `dotted` | `\"0.5,2.5\"` (round caps give circular dots) |\n| `dash-dot` | `\"5,2,1,2\"` |\n| `custom` | use `strokeDasharray` value verbatim |\n\n**SVG output**:\n```xml\n<line ... stroke-dasharray=\"5,3\" stroke-linecap=\"round\"/>\n<rect ... stroke-dasharray=\"0.5,2.5\" stroke-linecap=\"round\"/>\n```\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2)\n\n---\n\n### 2.3 Stroke Line Cap\n\n**Applies to**: line, path\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{ \"strokeLinecap\": \"round\" }\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Values |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `strokeLinecap` | string | `\"butt\"` | `\"butt\"`, `\"round\"`, `\"square\"` |\n\n**SVG output**: `stroke-linecap=\"round\"` on `<line>` or `<path>`.\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2) — required for dotted strokes to look correct.\n\n---\n\n### 2.4 Stroke Line Join\n\n**Applies to**: rect, path, polygon\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{ \"strokeLinejoin\": \"round\" }\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Values |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `strokeLinejoin` | string | `\"miter\"` | `\"miter\"`, `\"round\"`, `\"bevel\"` |\n| `strokeMiterlimit` | number | `4` | used with `\"miter\"` to avoid spiky corners |\n\n**SVG output**: `stroke-linejoin=\"round\"` on `<rect>` or `<path>`.\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2)\n\n---\n\n### 2.5 Arrow Heads\n\n**Applies to**: line, path\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"arrowStart\": \"none\",\n  \"arrowEnd\": \"arrow\"\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Values |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `arrowStart` | string | `\"none\"` | `\"none\"`, `\"arrow\"`, `\"arrow-open\"`, `\"dot\"`, `\"diamond\"` |\n| `arrowEnd` | string | `\"none\"` | same values |\n\n**SVG output** — uses `<marker>` defs:\n```xml\n<defs>\n  <marker id=\"arrow_end_e12\" markerWidth=\"10\" markerHeight=\"7\"\n          refX=\"10\" refY=\"3.5\" orient=\"auto\">\n    <polygon points=\"0 0, 10 3.5, 0 7\" fill=\"#000000\"/>\n  </marker>\n</defs>\n<line x1=\"...\" y1=\"...\" x2=\"...\" y2=\"...\"\n      stroke=\"#000000\" stroke-width=\"0.5\"\n      marker-end=\"url(#arrow_end_e12)\"/>\n```\n\nMarker fill color inherits from element's `stroke` color. Marker size scales proportionally to `strokeWidth`.\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2)\n\n---\n\n## 3. Shadow Effects\n\n### 3.1 Drop Shadow\n\n**Applies to**: all types (text, rect, line, circle, ellipse, image, path, group)\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"shadowX\": 3,\n  \"shadowY\": 3,\n  \"shadowBlur\": 5,\n  \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\"\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range / Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `shadowX` | number | `0` | mm, negative = left |\n| `shadowY` | number | `0` | mm, negative = up |\n| `shadowBlur` | number | `0` | mm, 0 = hard edge |\n| `shadowColor` | string | `\"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\"` | hex or rgba |\n\nShadow is disabled when `shadowX == 0 AND shadowY == 0 AND shadowBlur == 0`.\n\n**SVG output** — uses `<feDropShadow>` (simplest, widest support):\n```xml\n<defs>\n  <filter id=\"f_e7\" x=\"-20%\" y=\"-20%\" width=\"140%\" height=\"140%\">\n    <feDropShadow dx=\"3\" dy=\"3\" stdDeviation=\"2.5\"\n                  flood-color=\"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\" flood-opacity=\"1\"/>\n  </filter>\n</defs>\n<rect ... filter=\"url(#f_e7)\"/>\n```\n\nFilter region padding (`x=\"-20%\"` etc.) must be large enough to contain the shadow. A safe default is `max(shadowBlur, |shadowX|, |shadowY|) * 3` as a percentage of element size.\n\nAlternative using explicit primitives when combining with other filters:\n```xml\n<filter id=\"f_e7\">\n  <feGaussianBlur in=\"SourceAlpha\" stdDeviation=\"2.5\" result=\"blur\"/>\n  <feOffset dx=\"3\" dy=\"3\" result=\"offsetBlur\"/>\n  <feFlood flood-color=\"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\" result=\"color\"/>\n  <feComposite in=\"color\" in2=\"offsetBlur\" operator=\"in\" result=\"shadow\"/>\n  <feMerge>\n    <feMergeNode in=\"shadow\"/>\n    <feMergeNode in=\"SourceGraphic\"/>\n  </feMerge>\n</filter>\n```\n\nUse `<feDropShadow>` by default (simpler, single primitive). Fall back to the explicit chain only when compositing with other filter primitives in the same `<filter>` block.\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2) — already in baseline for image, extending to all types.\n\n---\n\n### 3.2 Inner Shadow\n\nFuture only. No spec yet.\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n## 4. Filter Effects\n\nFilters use SVG `<filter>` with `<feColorMatrix>` and `<feComponentTransfer>`. They are composited into a single `<filter>` block per element (one `<filter id=\"f_{id}\">` shared for shadow + image filters + blur).\n\n**Applies to**: image (primary use case), but architecturally available to all types.\n\n### 4.1 Brightness\n\n**Props JSONB**: `\"brightness\": 100`\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `brightness` | number | `100` | 0 (black) to 200 (2x bright). 100 = no change |\n\n**SVG filter primitive** (within `<feComponentTransfer>`):\n```xml\n<feComponentTransfer>\n  <feFuncR type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.2\" intercept=\"0\"/>\n  <feFuncG type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.2\" intercept=\"0\"/>\n  <feFuncB type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.2\" intercept=\"0\"/>\n</feComponentTransfer>\n```\n\n`slope = brightness / 100`. When combined with contrast: `slope = (brightness/100) * (contrast/100)`, `intercept = (1 - contrast/100) * 0.5`.\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2) — already in baseline for image.\n\n---\n\n### 4.2 Contrast\n\n**Props JSONB**: `\"contrast\": 100`\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `contrast` | number | `100` | 0 (gray) to 200 (2x contrast). 100 = no change |\n\nCombined with brightness in a single `<feComponentTransfer>`:\n- `slope = (brightness/100) * (contrast/100)`\n- `intercept = (1 - contrast/100) * 0.5`\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2) — already in baseline for image.\n\n---\n\n### 4.3 Grayscale\n\n**Props JSONB**: `\"grayscale\": 0`\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `grayscale` | number | `0` | 0 (full color) to 100 (full gray) |\n\n**SVG filter primitive**:\n```xml\n<feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\" values=\"0\"/>\n```\n\n`values = 1 - (grayscale / 100)`. `values=\"0\"` = fully desaturated, `values=\"1\"` = no change.\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2) — already in baseline for image.\n\n---\n\n### 4.4 Blur\n\n**Props JSONB**: `\"blur\": 0`\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `blur` | number | `0` | mm, 0 = no blur |\n\n**SVG filter primitive**:\n```xml\n<feGaussianBlur stdDeviation=\"2\"/>\n```\n\n`stdDeviation = blur` (in same coordinate units as the SVG, which is mm).\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3) — useful for background layers, frosted glass effects.\n\n---\n\n### 4.5 Sepia\n\n**Props JSONB**: `\"sepia\": 0`\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `sepia` | number | `0` | 0 to 100 |\n\n**SVG filter primitive** — compose a sepia `<feColorMatrix>` using type=\"matrix\" with the standard sepia matrix values, blended at `sepia/100` intensity:\n```xml\n<feColorMatrix type=\"matrix\" values=\"\n  0.393 0.769 0.189 0 0\n  0.349 0.686 0.168 0 0\n  0.272 0.534 0.131 0 0\n  0     0     0     1 0\"/>\n```\n\nFor partial sepia, interpolate each coefficient toward the identity matrix scaled by `sepia/100`.\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n### 4.6 Hue Rotate\n\n**Props JSONB**: `\"hueRotate\": 0`\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `hueRotate` | number | `0` | degrees, 0-360 |\n\n**SVG filter primitive**:\n```xml\n<feColorMatrix type=\"hueRotate\" values=\"180\"/>\n```\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n### 4.7 Saturate\n\n**Props JSONB**: `\"saturate\": 100`\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `saturate` | number | `100` | 0 (gray) to 200 (hyper-saturated). 100 = no change |\n\n**SVG filter primitive**:\n```xml\n<feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\" values=\"1.5\"/>\n```\n\n`values = saturate / 100`. This overlaps with grayscale (both use `type=\"saturate\"`). When both are set: `saturate` takes precedence if not 100, else `grayscale` applies. If both are non-default, apply grayscale first then saturate as a second matrix.\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n### 4.8 Filter Composition Rule\n\nAll active filters on a single element compile into **one `<filter>` block** in `<defs>`. The filter chain order is:\n\n1. Shadow (`feDropShadow` or explicit chain)\n2. Grayscale / saturate (`feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\"`)\n3. Hue rotate (`feColorMatrix type=\"hueRotate\"`)\n4. Sepia (`feColorMatrix type=\"matrix\"`)\n5. Brightness + Contrast combined (`feComponentTransfer`)\n6. Blur (`feGaussianBlur` at end so it blurs the already-color-corrected result)\n\nEach primitive uses `in=\"...\"` and `result=\"...\"` to chain. Final result feeds into `SourceGraphic` replacement. See section 10 for the full composited filter template.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Clip Effects\n\nClip paths are stored in `<defs>` as `<clipPath>` elements, referenced via `clip-path=\"url(#c_{id})\"`.\n\n### 5.1 Rectangular Clip with Border Radius\n\n**Applies to**: image, rect, group\n**Primary use case**: Rounding image corners\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"borderRadius\": 5\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `borderRadius` | number | `0` | mm, 0 = no rounding |\n\n**SVG output**:\n```xml\n<defs>\n  <clipPath id=\"c_e7\">\n    <rect x=\"20\" y=\"30\" width=\"60\" height=\"40\" rx=\"5\" ry=\"5\"/>\n  </clipPath>\n</defs>\n<image ... clip-path=\"url(#c_e7)\"/>\n```\n\nFor the image cover+crop case, the clip rect is positioned at `(el.x, el.y)` with `el.width x el.height`, same as the frame. The `<image>` element extends outside this rect and is clipped.\n\nPriority: MUST (Phase 1) — already in baseline for image cover mode.\n\n---\n\n### 5.2 Circular Clip\n\n**Applies to**: image, group\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"clipShape\": \"circle\"\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Values |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `clipShape` | string | `\"none\"` | `\"none\"`, `\"circle\"`, `\"rect\"` (rect = borderRadius clip) |\n\nWhen `clipShape = \"circle\"`, the clip radius is `min(width, height) / 2`, centered on the element.\n\n**SVG output**:\n```xml\n<defs>\n  <clipPath id=\"c_e7\">\n    <circle cx=\"50\" cy=\"50\" r=\"30\"/>\n  </clipPath>\n</defs>\n<image ... clip-path=\"url(#c_e7)\"/>\n```\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2)\n\n---\n\n### 5.3 Custom Path Clip\n\nFuture only.\n\n**Props JSONB sketch**:\n```json\n{\n  \"clipShape\": \"path\",\n  \"clipPath\": \"M10,10 L50,10 L50,50 Z\"\n}\n```\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n## 6. Transform Effects\n\n### 6.1 Rotation\n\n**Applies to**: all types\n\n**Props JSONB**: `\"rotation\": 0`\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `rotation` | number | `0` | degrees, -360 to 360. Positive = clockwise |\n\n**SVG output** — rotate around element center:\n```xml\n<rect ... transform=\"rotate(45, 50, 30)\"/>\n```\n\nWhere `(50, 30)` is `(x + width/2, y + height/2)` for rect/image/circle/ellipse, and `((x1+x2)/2, (y1+y2)/2)` for line. For groups, center is computed from the bounding box of all children.\n\nFor text: rotation center is `(x, y)` (the text anchor point), not a bounding box center, since text bbox requires font measurement.\n\nPriority: MUST (Phase 1) — already in baseline for all types.\n\n---\n\n### 6.2 Flip Horizontal / Vertical\n\n**Applies to**: image, text, group. Optionally rect/path.\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"flipH\": false,\n  \"flipV\": false\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `flipH` | boolean | `false` | Mirror left-right |\n| `flipV` | boolean | `false` | Mirror top-bottom |\n\n**SVG output** — translate-scale-translate around element center `(cx, cy)`:\n```xml\n<!-- flipH only -->\n<g transform=\"translate(cx,cy) scale(-1,1) translate(-cx,-cy)\">\n  <image .../>\n</g>\n\n<!-- both -->\n<g transform=\"translate(cx,cy) scale(-1,-1) translate(-cx,-cy)\">\n  <image .../>\n</g>\n```\n\nWhen combined with rotation: apply flip first (as inner transform), rotation second (as outer transform on the `<g>` or via separate `transform` attribute).\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2) — already in baseline for image.\n\n---\n\n### 6.3 Scale (future)\n\nNon-uniform scale is represented via explicit `width`/`height` changes, not a `scale` prop. Reserve `scaleX` / `scaleY` props for Phase 3 if needed.\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n## 7. Border Effects\n\nThe \"border\" category is specifically an overlay drawn on top of an element. It is distinct from `stroke` (which is SVG-native to shapes) because it is an explicit overlay rect — primarily designed for image borders but applicable to any framed element.\n\n### 7.1 Border Width, Color, Radius (Uniform)\n\n**Applies to**: image (primary), rect, group\n**Note for rect**: Use native `stroke`/`strokeWidth` for shape outlines. `borderWidth` is for the overlay pattern (drawn on top, inset to frame).\n\n**Props JSONB**:\n```json\n{\n  \"borderWidth\": 2,\n  \"borderColor\": \"#333333\",\n  \"borderRadius\": 5\n}\n```\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range / Notes |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `borderWidth` | number | `0` | mm. 0 = no border |\n| `borderColor` | string | `\"#000000\"` | hex or rgba |\n| `borderRadius` | number | `0` | mm. Applied to both clip and border rect |\n\n**SVG output** — overlay `<rect>` rendered after the element content:\n```xml\n<g>\n  <!-- image content with clip -->\n  <g clip-path=\"url(#c_e7)\">\n    <image .../>\n  </g>\n  <!-- border overlay -->\n  <rect x=\"20\" y=\"30\" width=\"60\" height=\"40\"\n        fill=\"none\"\n        stroke=\"#333333\"\n        stroke-width=\"2\"\n        rx=\"5\"/>\n</g>\n```\n\nThe border rect is drawn at the element's exact x/y/width/height. It is rendered after the image so it visually overlays the image edge. `fill=\"none\"` is required so the image shows through.\n\nWhen `borderRadius` is set and there is also a clip, both the `<clipPath><rect rx=.../>` and the overlay `<rect rx=.../>` use the same `borderRadius` value. This ensures clip and border align perfectly.\n\nPriority: SHOULD (Phase 2) — already in baseline for image.\n\n---\n\n### 7.2 Per-Corner Radius (future)\n\n**Props JSONB sketch**:\n```json\n{\n  \"borderRadiusTL\": 5,\n  \"borderRadiusTR\": 5,\n  \"borderRadiusBR\": 0,\n  \"borderRadiusBL\": 0\n}\n```\n\nRequires SVG `rx`/`ry` per-corner via a `<path>` rather than `<rect rx>`, since SVG 1.1 `<rect>` only supports uniform `rx`. SVG 2 supports separate `rx`/`ry` per corner, but browser/renderer support is inconsistent.\n\nImplementation: generate a `<path d=\"M ...\">` for the clip shape and border overlay.\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n## 8. Opacity and Blending\n\n### 8.1 Element Opacity\n\n**Applies to**: all types\n\n**Props JSONB**: `\"opacity\": 1`\n\n| Key | Type | Default | Range |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| `opacity` | number | `1` | 0.0 (invisible) to 1.0 (fully opaque) |\n\n**SVG output**: `opacity=\"0.5\"` attribute on the element or wrapping `<g>`.\n\nFor leaf elements: add directly to the element tag.\nFor groups: add to `<g opacity=\"0.5\">`.\nFor images with wrapping `<g>`: add to the outer `<g>`.\n\nPriority: MUST (Phase 1) — already in baseline for all types.\n\n---\n\n### 8.2 Blend Modes (future)\n\n**Props JSONB sketch**: `\"blendMode\": \"multiply\"`\n\n| Value | SVG attribute |\n|---|---|\n| `\"normal\"` | (default, no attribute) |\n| `\"multiply\"` | `mix-blend-mode: multiply` (CSS on element, not SVG attr) |\n| `\"screen\"` | `mix-blend-mode: screen` |\n| `\"overlay\"` | `mix-blend-mode: overlay` |\n| `\"darken\"` | `mix-blend-mode: darken` |\n| `\"lighten\"` | `mix-blend-mode: lighten` |\n| `\"color-dodge\"` | `mix-blend-mode: color-dodge` |\n\nSVG 2 / CSS: use `style=\"mix-blend-mode: multiply\"` on the element. Works in browsers for HTML+SVG, but may not render correctly in resvg / libsvg for PNG/PDF export. For export-safe blend modes, use `feBlend` filter primitive.\n\nPriority: COULD (Phase 3)\n\n---\n\n## 9. Applicability Matrix\n\nFor each effect category, which element types support it in the renderer:\n\n| Effect | text | rect | line | circle | ellipse | image | path | group |\n|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|\n| **Fill: solid** | Y (text color) | Y | — | Y | Y | — | Y | — |\n| **Fill: linear gradient** | Y | Y | — | Y | Y | — | Y | — |\n| **Fill: radial gradient** | Y | Y | — | Y | Y | — | Y | — |\n| **Fill: none** | Y | Y | — | Y | Y | — | Y | — |\n| **Stroke: solid** | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | — (use border) | Y | — |\n| **Stroke: dashed** | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | — | Y | — |\n| **Stroke: linecap** | — | — | Y | — | — | — | Y | — |\n| **Stroke: linejoin** | — | Y | — | — | — | — | Y | — |\n| **Arrow heads** | — | — | Y | — | — | — | Y | — |\n| **Shadow: drop** | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y |\n| **Filter: brightness** | — | — | — | — | — | Y | — | — |\n| **Filter: contrast** | — | — | — | — | — | Y | — | — |\n| **Filter: grayscale** | — | — | — | — | — | Y | — | — |\n| **Filter: blur** | Y | Y | — | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y |\n| **Filter: sepia** | — | — | — | — | — | Y | — | — |\n| **Filter: hue-rotate** | — | — | — | — | — | Y | — | — |\n| **Filter: saturate** | — | — | — | — | — | Y | — | — |\n| **Clip: rect+radius** | — | — | — | — | — | Y | — | Y |\n| **Clip: circle** | — | — | — | — | — | Y | — | Y |\n| **Transform: rotation** | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y |\n| **Transform: flip H/V** | Y | — | — | — | — | Y | Y | Y |\n| **Border: overlay** | — | — | — | — | — | Y | — | — |\n| **Opacity** | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y | Y |\n\n**Rationale for restrictions**:\n- Brightness/contrast/grayscale/sepia/hue-rotate/saturate: meaningful only on photographic content (image). Applying a color matrix to a solid-color rect is equivalent to just changing the fill color — the renderer should compute the resulting color and store it as a fill instead.\n- Stroke on image: images have no geometric stroke in SVG. The `borderWidth`/`borderColor` overlay serves this role.\n- Arrow heads: semantically meaningful only on open paths and lines.\n- Flip on rect: generally meaningless for symmetric shapes. Enable for path in Phase 2 if needed.\n\n---\n\n## 10. Composability: Combined Filter Chain\n\nWhen multiple filter effects are active on the same element, they compile into a single `<filter>` block. This is critical for correct rendering and performance.\n\n### 10.1 Filter ID Naming\n\nEach element gets a single filter: `id=\"f_{element_id}\"`. The filter is added to `<defs>` only when at least one effect requiring a filter is active.\n\nEffects requiring a `<filter>`:\n- Shadow (shadowBlur > 0 OR shadowX != 0 OR shadowY != 0)\n- Any image filter (brightness != 100 OR contrast != 100 OR grayscale != 0 OR blur != 0 OR sepia != 0 OR hueRotate != 0 OR saturate != 100)\n\nEffects NOT requiring a `<filter>` (direct SVG attributes):\n- Fill (attribute)\n- Stroke (attribute)\n- Opacity (attribute)\n- Rotation (transform attribute)\n- Flip (transform on wrapping `<g>`)\n\n### 10.2 Clip Path and Filter Interaction\n\nWhen both clip and filter are active on an image:\n- Clip is applied on the `<g>` wrapping the `<image>` content\n- Filter is applied on the `<image>` element itself (inside the clip)\n- This ensures the filter (including shadow) operates on the original unclipped image, while the visual result is clipped\n\n```xml\n<g opacity=\"0.9\" transform=\"rotate(5, cx, cy)\">\n  <g clip-path=\"url(#c_e7)\">\n    <image ... filter=\"url(#f_e7)\"/>\n  </g>\n  <rect ... fill=\"none\" stroke=\"#333\" stroke-width=\"2\" rx=\"5\"/>  <!-- border overlay -->\n</g>\n```\n\nShadow extends outside the clip by design (the shadow of a rounded-rect image should appear outside the clip boundary). If shadow should be clipped (shadow inside the clip), move `filter` to the outer `<g>` instead.\n\n### 10.3 Full Composited Filter Template\n\nThis is the canonical filter generation logic for an element with all effects active:\n\n```xml\n<filter id=\"f_e7\" x=\"-30%\" y=\"-30%\" width=\"160%\" height=\"160%\">\n\n  <!-- Step 1: Shadow (feDropShadow — simplest form) -->\n  <feDropShadow dx=\"3\" dy=\"3\" stdDeviation=\"2.5\"\n                flood-color=\"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\" flood-opacity=\"1\"\n                in=\"SourceGraphic\" result=\"withShadow\"/>\n\n  <!-- Step 2: Grayscale / Saturate (use result from step 1 as input) -->\n  <feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\" values=\"0.2\"\n                 in=\"withShadow\" result=\"desaturated\"/>\n\n  <!-- Step 3: Hue Rotate -->\n  <feColorMatrix type=\"hueRotate\" values=\"45\"\n                 in=\"desaturated\" result=\"hueShifted\"/>\n\n  <!-- Step 4: Brightness + Contrast combined -->\n  <feComponentTransfer in=\"hueShifted\" result=\"colorAdjusted\">\n    <feFuncR type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.1\" intercept=\"-0.05\"/>\n    <feFuncG type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.1\" intercept=\"-0.05\"/>\n    <feFuncB type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.1\" intercept=\"-0.05\"/>\n  </feComponentTransfer>\n\n  <!-- Step 5: Blur (last, blurs the fully-processed image) -->\n  <feGaussianBlur stdDeviation=\"1\" in=\"colorAdjusted\"/>\n\n</filter>\n```\n\nWhen shadow is combined with image filters, the shadow must be computed on `SourceGraphic` (original image) not on the color-corrected result. This requires splitting the chain:\n\n```xml\n<filter id=\"f_e7\">\n  <!-- Shadow from original -->\n  <feGaussianBlur in=\"SourceAlpha\" stdDeviation=\"2.5\" result=\"blur\"/>\n  <feOffset dx=\"3\" dy=\"3\" in=\"blur\" result=\"shadowOffset\"/>\n  <feFlood flood-color=\"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\" result=\"shadowColor\"/>\n  <feComposite in=\"shadowColor\" in2=\"shadowOffset\" operator=\"in\" result=\"shadow\"/>\n\n  <!-- Color corrections on SourceGraphic -->\n  <feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\" values=\"0.2\" in=\"SourceGraphic\" result=\"gray\"/>\n  <feComponentTransfer in=\"gray\" result=\"colorFinal\">\n    <feFuncR type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.1\" intercept=\"-0.05\"/>\n    <feFuncG type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.1\" intercept=\"-0.05\"/>\n    <feFuncB type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.1\" intercept=\"-0.05\"/>\n  </feComponentTransfer>\n\n  <!-- Merge: shadow behind corrected image -->\n  <feMerge>\n    <feMergeNode in=\"shadow\"/>\n    <feMergeNode in=\"colorFinal\"/>\n  </feMerge>\n</filter>\n```\n\n---\n\n## 11. Props JSONB Schema — Complete Per Element Type\n\nThese are the canonical JSONB shapes stored in `document.element.props`. Only non-default values need to be stored; the renderer applies defaults for missing keys.\n\n### 11.1 `image` element props\n\n```json\n{\n  \"objectFit\": \"cover\",\n  \"cropX\": 0.5,\n  \"cropY\": 0.5,\n  \"cropZoom\": 1,\n  \"flipH\": false,\n  \"flipV\": false,\n  \"brightness\": 100,\n  \"contrast\": 100,\n  \"grayscale\": 0,\n  \"blur\": 0,\n  \"sepia\": 0,\n  \"hueRotate\": 0,\n  \"saturate\": 100,\n  \"borderWidth\": 0,\n  \"borderColor\": \"#000000\",\n  \"borderRadius\": 0,\n  \"clipShape\": \"none\",\n  \"shadowX\": 0,\n  \"shadowY\": 0,\n  \"shadowBlur\": 0,\n  \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\"\n}\n```\n\n### 11.2 `rect` element props\n\n```json\n{\n  \"fill\": \"#000000\",\n  \"stroke\": \"none\",\n  \"strokeWidth\": 0,\n  \"strokeDash\": \"solid\",\n  \"strokeDasharray\": null,\n  \"strokeLinejoin\": \"miter\",\n  \"rx\": 0,\n  \"shadowX\": 0,\n  \"shadowY\": 0,\n  \"shadowBlur\": 0,\n  \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\",\n  \"gradient\": null\n}\n```\n\n### 11.3 `line` element props\n\n```json\n{\n  \"stroke\": \"#000000\",\n  \"strokeWidth\": 0.5,\n  \"strokeDash\": \"solid\",\n  \"strokeDasharray\": null,\n  \"strokeLinecap\": \"butt\",\n  \"arrowStart\": \"none\",\n  \"arrowEnd\": \"none\",\n  \"shadowX\": 0,\n  \"shadowY\": 0,\n  \"shadowBlur\": 0,\n  \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\"\n}\n```\n\n### 11.4 `circle` element props\n\n```json\n{\n  \"fill\": \"#000000\",\n  \"stroke\": \"none\",\n  \"strokeWidth\": 0,\n  \"strokeDash\": \"solid\",\n  \"shadowX\": 0,\n  \"shadowY\": 0,\n  \"shadowBlur\": 0,\n  \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\",\n  \"gradient\": null\n}\n```\n\n### 11.5 `ellipse` element props\n\nSame as `circle`.\n\n### 11.6 `text` element props\n\n```json\n{\n  \"fill\": \"#1C1C1C\",\n  \"stroke\": \"none\",\n  \"strokeWidth\": 0,\n  \"shadowX\": 0,\n  \"shadowY\": 0,\n  \"shadowBlur\": 0,\n  \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\",\n  \"gradient\": null\n}\n```\n\n### 11.7 `path` element props\n\n```json\n{\n  \"d\": \"M 0 0 L 100 100\",\n  \"fill\": \"none\",\n  \"stroke\": \"#000000\",\n  \"strokeWidth\": 0.5,\n  \"strokeDash\": \"solid\",\n  \"strokeDasharray\": null,\n  \"strokeLinecap\": \"butt\",\n  \"strokeLinejoin\": \"miter\",\n  \"arrowStart\": \"none\",\n  \"arrowEnd\": \"none\",\n  \"shadowX\": 0,\n  \"shadowY\": 0,\n  \"shadowBlur\": 0,\n  \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\",\n  \"gradient\": null\n}\n```\n\n### 11.8 `group` element props\n\n```json\n{\n  \"clipShape\": \"none\",\n  \"shadowX\": 0,\n  \"shadowY\": 0,\n  \"shadowBlur\": 0,\n  \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\"\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## 12. Full Example: Image with All Effects Active\n\nThe question prompt's example, with all keys specified:\n```json\n{\n  \"objectFit\": \"cover\",\n  \"cropX\": 0.5,\n  \"cropY\": 0.5,\n  \"cropZoom\": 1,\n  \"flipH\": false,\n  \"flipV\": false,\n  \"brightness\": 110,\n  \"contrast\": 95,\n  \"grayscale\": 20,\n  \"blur\": 0,\n  \"sepia\": 0,\n  \"hueRotate\": 0,\n  \"saturate\": 100,\n  \"borderWidth\": 2,\n  \"borderColor\": \"#333333\",\n  \"borderRadius\": 5,\n  \"clipShape\": \"none\",\n  \"shadowX\": 3,\n  \"shadowY\": 3,\n  \"shadowBlur\": 5,\n  \"shadowColor\": \"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\"\n}\n```\n\nGenerated SVG for this element (id `e7`, at x=20mm, y=30mm, 60x40mm):\n\n```xml\n<defs>\n  <clipPath id=\"c_e7\">\n    <rect x=\"20\" y=\"30\" width=\"60\" height=\"40\" rx=\"5\"/>\n  </clipPath>\n  <filter id=\"f_e7\" x=\"-25%\" y=\"-25%\" width=\"150%\" height=\"150%\">\n    <feGaussianBlur in=\"SourceAlpha\" stdDeviation=\"2.5\" result=\"blur\"/>\n    <feOffset dx=\"3\" dy=\"3\" in=\"blur\" result=\"shadowOff\"/>\n    <feFlood flood-color=\"rgba(0,0,0,0.4)\" result=\"shadowCol\"/>\n    <feComposite in=\"shadowCol\" in2=\"shadowOff\" operator=\"in\" result=\"shadow\"/>\n    <feColorMatrix type=\"saturate\" values=\"0.8\" in=\"SourceGraphic\" result=\"gray\"/>\n    <feComponentTransfer in=\"gray\" result=\"colorFinal\">\n      <feFuncR type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.045\" intercept=\"0.025\"/>\n      <feFuncG type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.045\" intercept=\"0.025\"/>\n      <feFuncB type=\"linear\" slope=\"1.045\" intercept=\"0.025\"/>\n    </feComponentTransfer>\n    <feMerge>\n      <feMergeNode in=\"shadow\"/>\n      <feMergeNode in=\"colorFinal\"/>\n    </feMerge>\n  </filter>\n</defs>\n\n<g>\n  <g clip-path=\"url(#c_e7)\">\n    <!-- cover crop: imgW/H computed from naturalWidth/Height and cropZoom -->\n    <g>\n      <image x=\"18.5\" y=\"29\" width=\"63\" height=\"42\"\n             href=\"data:image/png;base64,...\"\n             preserveAspectRatio=\"none\"\n             filter=\"url(#f_e7)\"/>\n    </g>\n  </g>\n  <!-- border overlay on top of clip -->\n  <rect x=\"20\" y=\"30\" width=\"60\" height=\"40\"\n        fill=\"none\" stroke=\"#333333\" stroke-width=\"2\" rx=\"5\"/>\n</g>\n```\n\nFilter coefficient computation for brightness=110, contrast=95, grayscale=20:\n- `sat_value = 1 - 20/100 = 0.8`\n- `slope = (110/100) * (95/100) = 1.1 * 0.95 = 1.045`\n- `intercept = (1 - 95/100) * 0.5 = 0.05 * 0.5 = 0.025`\n\n---\n\n## 13. Build Sequence (Implementation Phases)\n\n### Phase 1 — MUST (Core rendering, matches existing baseline + new types)\n\n- [ ] Solid fill on all fill-capable types (rect, circle, ellipse, path, text)\n- [ ] Fill `\"none\"` support\n- [ ] Solid stroke on all stroke-capable types\n- [ ] Element opacity on all types\n- [ ] Rotation on all types (using bounding box center)\n- [ ] Rectangular clip with border radius for image cover mode\n- [ ] Drop shadow on image (via `<feDropShadow>`)\n- [ ] Brightness + contrast + grayscale filter on image\n- [ ] Border overlay on image\n- [ ] Flip H/V on image (translate-scale-translate)\n- [ ] Filter ID generation and `<defs>` accumulation in `render_svg`\n\n### Phase 2 — SHOULD (Professional quality)\n\n- [ ] Drop shadow extended to all types (not just image)\n- [ ] Dashed / dotted stroke with presets\n- [ ] Stroke linecap (butt, round, square)\n- [ ] Stroke linejoin (miter, round, bevel)\n- [ ] Arrow heads on line and path via `<marker>` defs\n- [ ] Linear gradient fill (rect, circle, ellipse, path, text)\n- [ ] Circular clip for image\n- [ ] Border overlay extended to group\n- [ ] Flip H/V extended to text and group\n- [ ] Blur filter on any type\n- [ ] Text stroke (outline text effect)\n- [ ] Combined filter chain (shadow + color filters in single `<filter>`)\n\n### Phase 3 — COULD (Advanced / future)\n\n- [ ] Radial gradient fill\n- [ ] Pattern fill (hatching, dots)\n- [ ] Sepia, hue-rotate, saturate filters\n- [ ] Per-corner border radius (using path instead of rect in clipPath)\n- [ ] Custom path clip\n- [ ] Blend modes (mix-blend-mode)\n- [ ] Inner shadow\n- [ ] Non-uniform scale (scaleX/scaleY)\n\n---\n\n## 14. Critical Implementation Notes for `document.render_svg`\n\n**Defs accumulation**: The PL/pgSQL renderer must accumulate all `<defs>` entries (filters, clip paths, gradient defs, markers) across all elements before emitting the SVG. Use a JSONB array or text array within the function, deduplicated by `id`. Emit all defs in a single `<defs>` block before the element body.\n\n**Filter region sizing**: SVG filters require explicit region declarations (`x`, `y`, `width`, `height` on `<filter>`). Use `x=\"-20%\" y=\"-20%\" width=\"140%\" height=\"140%\"` as a safe default. For large shadows, compute: `padding_pct = max(|shadowX|, |shadowY|, shadowBlur * 3) / element_size * 100 + 10`.\n\n**Coordinate system**: All coordinates are in mm (the SVG `viewBox` and `width`/`height` are in mm). SVG filter `stdDeviation` values are in the same coordinate space — no DPI conversion needed at this layer. DPI scaling happens at export time (PNG snapshot, PDF).\n\n**ID uniqueness**: Every element generates at most one `<clipPath>` (id `c_{element_id}`) and one `<filter>` (id `f_{element_id}`) and one or two `<marker>` (id `arrow_start_{element_id}`, `arrow_end_{element_id}`). IDs use the element's database ID, which is globally unique within a document.\n\n**No `stroke` on `image`**: The SVG `<image>` element does not support `stroke`. The border overlay pattern (explicit `<rect fill=\"none\" stroke=...>`) is the correct approach and must be maintained for image borders.\n\n**`feDropShadow` vs explicit chain**: Use `feDropShadow` when shadow is the only filter. Switch to the explicit `feGaussianBlur + feOffset + feFlood + feComposite + feMerge` chain when combining shadow with color filters (brightness, contrast, grayscale). This ensures the shadow is cast from the original un-color-corrected source alpha.\n\n**Gradient orientation**: Store gradient `angle` in degrees (0=bottom-to-top, 90=left-to-right). Compute SVG `(x1,y1,x2,y2)` using `gradientUnits=\"objectBoundingBox\"` for simplicity. Formula: given angle `θ`, `x1 = 0.5 - 0.5*cos(θ_rad)`, `y1 = 0.5 + 0.5*sin(θ_rad)`, `x2 = 1 - x1`, `y2 = 1 - y1`.\n\n**Color parsing**: Accept hex (`#rgb`, `#rrggbb`, `#rrggbbaa`), `rgb(r,g,b)`, `rgba(r,g,b,a)`, and CSS named colors. Normalize to `rgba` internally for `flood-color` in SVG filter attributes since some SVG renderers (resvg) handle `rgba()` in `flood-color` correctly but may not handle hex with alpha.\n\n---\n\n## 15.
